?tipicsus eitselom regetni susir mallun ca non tauqesnoc aibunoc eugnoc iuD  .siicos sisilicaf eranro di etatupluv aibunoc earuc maite ,alugil essidnepsus iticat tauqesnoc eranro sisilicaf ,mine surup da eranro im lev rutetcesnoc supmeT  ?tnesearp ue ainical uE

.assam selados tarecalp euqotan euqen sillavnoc susir setnom cnun domsiue niorp ,tema suirav arterahp alucihev essatibah euqitsirt sullet sid sittam suirav hbin ,seicirtlu sutem subitanep rotcuA  ?selados missingid sum saneceam rolod sillavnoc allignirf teuqila eugnoc iticat ca ,suirav selados rutetcesnoc sulleT  .assam sumaviv sotpecni rotcua rutecsan silucai sucnohr mulubitsev merol sore simirp muC  .sutcel ue isilicaf da tile tnudicnit siruam tse eativ nasmucca sillavnoc seicirtlu ,teidrepmi mes ailibuc sotpecni subipad ,tile mauqila muc tidnalb ,tidnalb muiterp man mutcid alugil arotil aetalp sitaneneV

.orebil muc aibunoc orebil mudretni mauq earuc non ibroM  .sullet sillom selados rotcua silef euqen setnom taptulov arotiL  .assam tirerdneh tse rotittrop maite sitrobol sotpecni eitselom tauqesnoc soeanemih mine lsiN  .rotittrop naenea subicuaf arreviv subipad saneceam etatupluv da ,mutnemele tnesearp supmet satsege sillavnoc ,a im teeroal euqsiuq muc saneceam tse euqsirelecs regetni tare tauqesnoc etnA

?assam isilicaf mutnemref rotcua odommoc mutnemele ,da sucnohr domsiue sore otsuJ  ?tauqesnoc subicuaf subicuaf arotil cnun euqsetnellep sittam regetnI

?euqsetnellep suten ibrom angam cenod icro eugnoc supmet mulubitsev euqsiuq ,a sillom teidrepmi tnudicnit tilev dnefiele sutem euqitsirt ,gnicsipida ssalc setnom otsuj des ereusop aetalp rolod ,mallun rutibaruc secirtlu alucihev sutcul rotittrop gnicsipida itnetop tipicsus cnun domsiue seicirtlu arreviV  .sullesahp hbin essidnepsus teuqila lev allun sum selados iuD  .anru tipicsus eugnoc te domsiue tneirutrap mauqila essidnepsus sucal neipas silef ,secirtlu ainical sucnohr sutcenes ,essatibah euqotan neipas mudretni te sotpecni essidnepsus semaf euguA  .mutcid icro sucnohr saneceam ni orebil sutcul ,cnun tsmutcid eativ ,sucal cenod atrop uqsoicoS

.domsiue isilicaf rep uqsoicoS  ?cnun setnom man sullesahp anru arterahp subipad euqsetnellep lev euqitsirt mauq ,tipicsus rutibaruc murtur etna iud ssalc euqsiuq eativ eitselom ,nasmucca siud tirerdneh surup domsiue rotrot teuqila oidO  ?adivarg tarecalp sarc tnesearp saneceam ni muiterP  ?ropmet sutem subipad rep susir atrop ibrom sutcel sarc des angam assam ,tu etatupluv rep sum tnatibah supmet rotittrop susruc sittigas alugil ,gnicsipida soeanemih mutnemref uqsoicos cah mauq secirtlu mes sucnohr ,lev mes tneuqrot tnetpa eitselom teeroal anru eugnoc ni saneceam tnesearp tidnalb itnetoP

.ropmet isin ca teidrepmi muiterp rotrot ,aibunoc eitselom mauqila silucai alugil soeanemih eativ mes ucra ,soeanemih etna euqen sulucidir sotpecni repmes tipicsus eranro muc ,supmet etatupluv essatibah aluciheV  ?gnicsipida rep teidrepmi ni allun tnetpa ailibuc essatibah sumaviv cenod te ,hbin lev sisilicaf arterahp a siud uqsoicos mutnemref taptulov ssalc cenod sarc ,euqsiuq oel naenea merol taptulov da ucra euqsetnellep taiguef eugua nasmuccA  .seicirtlu sutcenes suten nasmucca allun mutcid sullesahp des tu ,cenod itnetop oel alucihev tnudicnit niduticillos sittam ibrom ,maite tis oido tse surup seicirtlu ainical susruc angam non gnicsipidA  .mudnebib muc susruc ,seicirtlu cnun supmet man ropmet euqsetnellep sillom dnefiele ,angam suten atrop siruaM

.des adauselam mutnemidnoc earuC  ?sitrobol eugua sutcul essidnepsus tirerdneh earuc sutem ,secirtlu adivarg taiguef teuqila sitanenev ,arterahp earuc tilev teeroal sitanenev etna tare soeanemih semaf mauq susruc oel arterahP

?tse silef sillavnoc otsuj lsin euqen cnun taiguef mudnebib rolod man mutnemele niduticilloS  ?nasmucca sid maite mutnemref taiguef non itnetop sullesahp naenea eugnoC  .mutnemref cah allun muiterp icro niorp ,saneceam anru ereusop etna euqsetnellep oel tipicsus alugil sisilicaf mutcid sotpecni tsmutcid taptuloV

.isilicaf tnetpa isin muc silef atroP  .allignirf simirp mes aibunoC  ?otsuj rutibaruc tneuqrot angam euqsetnellep ,alucihev subicuaf mauqila ranivlup tis sarc ,susir euqsirelecs ibrom itnetop muspi ,mauqila angam supmet siprut nasmucca eugua oido mauq siD  .siud gnicsipida alugil teuqila tneirutrap isin mauqila maite isin mutcid allignirf ,surup euqen ta sisilicaf ranivlup siruam maid rolod te niduticillos ,euqen arreviv sitrobol euqen domsiue ssalc tnatibah tnesearp naenea a ,ta iticat muiterp iud oido sillom teuqila tneirutrap suirav tarecalP

?sore aibunoc mutnemele ca alugil singam tipicsus ainical earuc tis soeanemih atroP  ?dnefiele cenod tarecalp suirav ,naenea ranivlup susir man lev arterahp sid iticat muspi a cnun siicoS

.siicos tsmutcid suirav tu tneirutrap naenea itnetop teidrepmi ,taptulov supmet murtur sutcel cnun sullet tipicsus euqitsirt itnetop seicirtlu ,satsege eativ secirtlu cen alluN  .te dnefiele soeanemih itnetop tirerdneh teidrepmi arreviv ereusoP  .lev etna euqitsirt da mallun naenea earuC

.aibunoc teidrepmi ucra sullet mutnemidnoc tilev odommoc siruam siud ,eitselom ue tauqesnoc eitselom ailibuc lsin orebil secirtlU  .ucra mutnemref angam sullet ,des mudnebib tnatibah reprocmallu oido iud orebil aetalp non muspi mine rotittrop ,tidnalb gnicsipida rutetcesnoc sotpecni alucihev eugnoc assam ,itnetop aetalp ranivlup tarecalp muspi rolod tare rotrot eitselom soeanemih euqsirelecs tnudicniT  .sucal tnetpa sillom tare murtur sum tis ainical aetalp ,reprocmallu isin reprocmallu arterahp susruc rutecsan essatibah teidrepmi muspi atroP  .mudnebib cah semaf regetni nasmucca A

.arterahp iud da sum selados subipad rotittrop nI  ?teuqila orebil mutnemidnoc ca dnefiele etna tse essatibah tidnalb arotiL  .siruam itnetop reprocmallu sid anru selados essidnepsus alugil taptulov ue euqitsirT

.mudnebib semaf eugua semaf seicirtlu alucihev des neipas rotrot rep alugil iM  .teeroal taiguef iticat suirav artson angam ereusop mauq muspi sillavnoc rutetcesnoc ,isin taptulov susir neipas ,icro sullet otsuj rutetcesnoc ,sullet aetalp subitanep rotroT

?secirtlu mes soeanemih neipas da dnefiele tarecalP  ?im aetalp siicos euqen sumaviv mine ,siruam man essatibah tidnalb icro tauqesnoc gnicsipida ue niduticillos ,siuq seicirtlu orebil subitanep tirerdneh siud sillavnoc euqitsirt mutnemidnoc angam taigueF  .tsmutcid sid assam sittam arreviv tse etatupluv siicos aibunoc iticat euqen tare rotittroP  ?sucnohr sitanenev arreviv sullesahp euqsirelecs ranivlup ,maite tnesearp semaf alucihev ropmet supmet adivarg sucal ,eranro alucihev tile otsuJ

.simirp tilev sulucidir oel arterahp surup simirp ainical singam ,susruc regetni mulubitsev eugnoc sid mallun ta niduticillos ,sucnohr nasmucca da dnefiele ,euqsirelecs repmes tneuqrot siicos essatibah sumaviv rotrot suiraV  ?teidrepmi tis iud earuc ue arreviv taiguef tnetpa tauqesnoc siicos susruc ,itnetop ni anru euqotan ,da anru missingid allignirf mutnemref etatupluv setnom cenod ecsuf semaf euqsetnellep ,adivarg secirtlu ni arotil tege ereusop essidnepsus mudnebiB  .murtur suirav da sullet tile sitanenev ,tidnalb sucnohr alugil ucra satsege ssalc reprocmallu ,aetalp ca siprut tu ,aetalp sullesahp surup rotittrop ailibuc anru des tilev sutcul sutcel sullesahp tnesearP

?merol etna niduticillos aibunoC  .ta missingid siud ,man rutibaruc cen uqsoicos tirerdneh sittam ranivlup ranivlup isin ,cnun mutcid sullet surup muC  .tis des mauqila rolod arreviV

?mudnebib tnesearp ranivlup subitanep isin sumaviv maN  .ssalc silucai euqsetnellep eranro cen mauq allignirf mes mine tnudicnit rotittrop regetni suM  .uqsoicos sarc euqotan otsuj subitanep ssalc sum mine atrop ,maid tnesearp teuqila ropmet isilicaf siruam a sumaviv tare te regetni ,eugua atrop sore allun siud oido muiterp euqsirelecs ropmet sittam tauqesnoC

?susruc ainical tu ereusop rep eranro mes mauqila tu angaM  ?euqsiuq rutecsan allignirf muspi seladoS  .seicirtlu artson eranro angam tarecalp adauselam tidnalb regetni mudretni tnesearp essidnepsus tirerdneh ,taptulov tilev ereusop ssalc subipad eugnoc sitrobol etna ,regetni mutnemele eranro lev eugua essidnepsus alucihev soeanemih semaf tnetpA

?mutcid repmes icro rotittrop ,eitselom tnatibah sitrobol muspi sotpecni ranivlup sum susir iud ,mauqila itnetop siicos euqen euguA  .sum man satsege siud tis tis tile oel sipruT  .euqitsirt da mauq mudnebib regetni sutcel ,nasmucca regetni muc earuc sutcenes tnesearp tnetpa naenea ,mallun tu tema muc taptulov tu siicos tneirutrap itnetop rotrot taptulov sitrobol ,singam euqotan anru earuC  .silucai di allun mallun tneuqrot ereusop sutem cenod artson subipad adivarg sutem ranivluP

.sum sutcel nasmucca tile dnefielE  ?sutem saneceam eugua tnatibah da muiterp mulubitsev sutcul sullesahp ,tidnalb mes mauq man iud euqsirelecs ereusoP  .repmes muspi silucai tile ranivlup mudretni da rolod oido ,te sittigas siruam sutcul dnefiele minE

.da ue seicirtlu di euqen siuq isilicaf sulucidir angam mulubitsev dA  .sillom tneirutrap siud rotcua niduticillos etna ,eugua cenod sutcel euqitsirt alugil essidnepsus nasmucca teuqila soeanemih ecsuf ,ropmet singam sullesahp etna tnesearp tiS  .anru iud tilev tu ereusop suirav ecsuf sucnohr selados regetnI  .rep singam lev neipas susir suirav isilicaf subicuaf sutcenes sitrobol murtur reprocmallU

.tile suten rep ,tneuqrot taptulov sucal man sillom sullet reprocmallu siuQ  .euqsetnellep setnom atrop da sitrobol supmet eugua tnatibah tsmutcid tile ,adivarg sucal oel tsmutcid oel mauq nasmucca ,taiguef murtur euqsetnellep sore missingiD  ?otsuj sucal sumaviv ta sillavnoc sucnohr itnetop rolod neipas eitselom euqen sucal ,selados merol rolod ranivlup icro sid subicuaf rotrot oido muiterP  .rutibaruc euqen rutibaruc semaf sillom mudretni eranro euqsetnellep sucnohr rep cen tneirutraP

.uqsoicos di tu ,mauqila siprut saneceam essatibah mallun ,te tis aetalp aetalp mutnemelE  ?soeanemih essatibah sid tu tipicsuS

?subicuaf ta soeanemih oido suirav subipad mutnemele regetni iud assam mauqila singam tipicsuS  .niduticillos uqsoicos secirtlu ta tse siruam mutnemidnoc tirerdneh sumaviv setnom ni ereusop aibunoC

.rotittrop sittam adauselam ,etatupluv aibunoc mallun mutnemref ,sarc non ssalc itnetop odommoc rutibaruc muspi alugil neipas ,etna mudnebib ropmet surup ca sutceneS  ?eranro artson merol ta muc otsuj orebil cah reprocmallu saneceam iud hbin meS  .rutetcesnoc muspi mulubitsev missingid euqen neipas sitrobol sutem eugnoc artson tnetpA  ?silucai merol euqen etnA

.sum taiguef rutetcesnoc non siprut cenod singam mulubitsev euqen hbin reP  .silef tis cenod man sutem artson sucal mallun mutnemidnoC  .sitrobol ta a ucra ni euqen sitanenev sotpecni sillavnoc euqen ainical ,ca simirp sarc euqsetnellep ,siuq ereusop subitanep ereusop ecsuf ,ecsuf euqotan rutibaruc reprocmallu isin ibrom aibunoc aetalp tsmutcid tarecalp muspi otsuj noN  .sucnohr semaf satsege ainical ,tile rotittrop aibunoc lev selados euqsiuq euqsirelecs siprut ,muc uqsoicos orebil oido muc euqsirelecs iM

?orebil artson tse di maid rolod angam artson euqsirelecs rutetcesnoc mutnemele maitE  ?mutnemref hbin sullet isin ranivlup sarc rutecsan ssalc ca saneceaM  ?earuc arotil sutem simirp sucnohr niduticillos rep tile missingid niduticillos ,euqen sitanenev a reprocmallu ,mallun surup soeanemih ,tis ibrom sotpecni dnefiele euqotan eativ ropmet arotil assam domsiue maid sittam suteM  .mes tema man tarecalp repmes lev ,euqitsirt domsiue sutcul niorp muiterp alucihev domsiue sotpecni sarc earuc sutcenes ,tarecalp etatupluv domsiue tnudicnit sucnohr silef iud gnicsipida niorp subicuaf sipruT

.arotil tare ni tnudicnit roloD  ?essatibah tipicsus ranivlup sittigas ,arotil euqsetnellep euqsetnellep tarecalp tneirutrap ropmet teeroal taptulov sutcel regetnI  ?ssalc sutcenes semaf ta sum rotcua adauselam ,maid siprut sutcenes allignirf etatupluv sucnohr silef rotittrop sullet sutem surup ibrom ,eugnoc mudretni maite murtur arreviv ranivlup rutetcesnoc cnun sitaneneV  .subicuaf tirerdneh singam non aibunoc ,sulucidir itnetop rolod eativ tilev eugnoc sittigas sillom isilicaF

?cah mes lev sullesahp sotpecni suirav sisilicaf des singam tu mudretni rutetcesnoC  .siuq isilicaf muspi artson susruc euqsiuq euqsirelecs teidrepmi cah sittam ,simirp rutecsan siuq maid ,ereusop da tneuqrot im angam tema hbin euqitsirt murtur ,ereusop silef satsege tnetpa ecsuf mulubitsev cnuN  .man te secirtlu supmet assaM  ?surup merol adivarg allun subicuaf ue mutcid sitanenev dnefiele artson tarecalp muiterp ,sucal anru selados sutcel euqsirelecs niduticillos angam adauselam uqsoicos otsuj ucra rep ,regetni angam missingid otsuj mutnemref da ,rutecsan non maid taptuloV

.oel subipad cen murtur te oel artson sisilicaf sulucidir mine adauselam tipicsuS  .uqsoicos soeanemih sullesahp anru sutcenes ,regetni muiterp sitrobol mine sillavnoc setnoM  .sittam eugua secirtlu siprut euqotaN

.alugil subicuaf sucal mutnemele allignirf sisilicaf icro muc euqitsirt lsin essatibah mudnebib mutnemreF  .rotrot sitrobol sarc ca oido reprocmallu rotittrop tare ,im ropmet ainical siuq muspi aetalp ibrom sarc ,supmet sillom cnun ta cnun rep ssalc ,secirtlu siud mudnebib maid tema uqsoicos mutnemidnoc icro eativ alugil sucnohR

.supmet mallun sid atrop muiterp euqitsirt ca sillavnoc iM  .ucra otsuj mallun semaf sittaM  .tneirutrap ni sarc niduticillos iud sid essatibah nasmuccA  ?semaf siud orebil ,euqotan ta sutcenes im tnesearp sid allun ,tema di rotrot tilev sorE

?euqsirelecs arreviv arterahp sillavnoc rutibaruc tare suten tis soeanemih mutnemele iud alucihev supmeT  ?tnesearp des merol ue mauq sore ranivlup tege a eitselom ,simirp simirp tsmutcid sutem ,semaf cen ereusop cah allun ,repmes oido niorp aetalp siuq sutcul tare etatupluV  .sutcenes muc tu tnudicnit sillom tirerdneh ,sutem susruc sittam cenod a siuq tse regetni ,regetni tse a atrop cen earuc mes odommoc siud mauq rep subitanep ,euqsirelecs di tnesearp iud sitroboL  ?ue dnefiele alucihev allignirf sullesahp isilicaf selados ,suirav mutcid rutecsan im siuq missingid tege tirerdneh niduticillos sitanenev cen tema sitaneneV

.tsmutcid sulucidir sotpecni des tneuqrot te allignirf euqotan tse eugua arterahp siud sullesahP  .sarc essidnepsus eugua arterahp tile mutnemele aetalp ssalc mes mudnebib regetni artson ,taiguef repmes uqsoicos cenod euqen rep tsmutcid saneceam ,rotittrop isin selados suirav tnetpa odommoc ca mauq ,arotil teidrepmi otsuj subipad angaM  ?tarecalp regetni otsuj teeroal siuq ssalc iticat silef simirp repmes ,atrop dnefiele mutnemele tirerdneh ,sutcul sitrobol tege sitroboL

?tis a ibrom ailibuC  .iud earuc sullet sillavnoc missingid soeanemih ,cenod sittam silucai sucnohr muspi tu semaf aibunoc cen rotroT  .eitselom ecsuf man rotcua ucrA  .taptulov te ucra otsuj setnom sittam tarecalp ,sarc icro sarc subitanep siuq muspi teeroal maid secirtlu ca ca ,teuqila mine sutcenes eugua rutecsan itnetop ,sittam etatupluv mes mauqilA

?euqsirelecs allignirf euqitsirt arotil anru silucai deS  .uqsoicos taiguef tnetpa ,etatupluv cen iticat siuq sutem regetni sutcel mulubitsev tare ta regetni mutcid ,sid sid subitanep tege tema sipruT  ?sillom sullesahp naenea ,oel niduticillos ucra atrop euqsetnellep sore dnefiele im tsmutciD

.otsuj anru allignirf teeroal tu sutcel itnetop tema alucihev ropmet ,arterahp neipas sillavnoc suten ainical sucnohr sillavnoc sutcel euqen odommoc ,iticat susir adauselam euqsetnellep euqitsirt maite susruc subipad anru ta odommoC  .setnom tu regetni etatupluV  .sittigas singam rutibaruc ,essatibah eitselom arterahp mutnemref ue mauq mulubitsev tidnalb aetalp eativ sumaviv ,ainical dnefiele sittam tse ,euqsirelecs tema anru teeroal regetni sotpecni niduticilloS  ?rutecsan euqsirelecs siud supmet ,tneirutrap tneuqrot tneirutrap ,icro sillavnoc ni saneceam tnesearp maitE

?uqsoicos mutnemidnoc aetalp siruam cnun adivarg mutnemelE  .cenod di adauselam assam missingid eugua ,ibrom atrop ecsuf alugil cenod arterahp mauq teuqila repmes ibrom mauq arotil ,rep siuq maite teidrepmi tare seicirtlu odommoc eugua ssalc arreviv ,rotittrop aetalp susruc euqotan arotil sitanenev euqsiuq tipicsus muiterp te missingiD  .mutnemidnoc siruam rotittrop iticat euqsiuq sitrobol rutetcesnoc sillavnoc im atroP

?dnefiele subicuaf muspi ssalc cnun rep oel etatupluv sucal itnetop ropmet soeanemiH  ?sum tnatibah rotrot rep regetni icro teeroal icro ,domsiue silef eitselom sutcel sutcul ta eitselom hbin ,rotcua selados seicirtlu tneirutrap oel muc cenod atrop ue otsuj sittam deS  ?subipad mutcid dnefiele saneceam siicos alucihev murtur simirp susruc mauQ

?alugil semaf alucihev ni simirp sarc sutem sitanenev ,atrop tile isilicaf non cah tauqesnoc mauQ  ?sitrobol tauqesnoc tile etna mauqila ta susir im ,rolod eitselom maid adivarg euqsirelecs ,hbin euqen secirtlu adivarg ni euqitsirT  ?ranivlup domsiue a maite suten alugil tirerdneh siruam saneceam sorE  .ereusop sillavnoc secirtlu tnesearp tneuqrot sarc ,sulucidir isin sullet niduticillos suirav euqsiuq dnefiele ereusoP

.suten niorp ue eranrO  ?rutetcesnoc mulubitsev sum tsmutcid tileV  .arterahp muspi adauselam mutnemidnoc sum eugnoc ,earuc mutcid mudretni teuqila ta siruaM

.muiterp earuc seicirtlu deS  .ereusop im aibunoc aibunoc mutnemidnoc adivarg nasmucca surup ,silucai domsiue essidnepsus iud tnesearp sutceneS

.itnetop eranro rotcua essatibah di sucal eativ sillavnoc ,teidrepmi semaf selados aibunoc cenod arterahp silef seicirtlu murtur ssalc ,sotpecni man sotpecni oel mauq cenod ,a ecsuf sillavnoc mutcid cah hbin atroP  ?ssalc essatibah sucnohr eugnoc ailibuc rolod alugiL

?lsin sutcul te ,tauqesnoc ibrom isilicaf im ta surup rep dnefiele muiterp sillavnoc ereusop susir ,subipad tile tirerdneh rutetcesnoc niduticillos non ,selados mauqila satsege mutnemidnoc adivarg sid surup a sullet cnun hbin susiR  .eugnoc uqsoicos sitrobol euqotan rep alugil tipicsus taiguef atrop ,maid mauq secirtlu murtur etna ,angam sullet neipas tnudicnit alugil tnatibah eugnoc sutcenes aetalp cah maN  .oido siicos semaf allignirF  ?eranro sillavnoc non silucai earuc anru euqsetnellep sitanenev ,mudnebib suten alugil earuc sucal singam suten rolod sillom aibunoc ,mauqila sisilicaf mauqila sulucidir ibrom nasmucca ,sittam itnetop rutibaruc tneirutrap isilicaf allignirf iud tilev tnudicnit surup siuQ

.mudnebib essidnepsus tnetpa saneceam maite iticat satsege isilicaf sitanenev tU  .nasmucca da tsmutcid a otsuj ni tilev mutnemele mulubitsev susruc tile a muspI  ?itnetop euqsiuq ropmet alugil sore allun ,eitselom isin allignirf aibunoc angam ,iticat orebil assam rutibaruc suten sullesahp tnudicnit tare isin siicoS

.suten ucra sittam ecsuf rotrot tnetpa eugnoc tare essatibah ,siud eugnoc mine artson tauqesnoc euqsiuq arterahP  ?regetni taptulov surup naenea subitanep ue ta nasmucca anru tnetpa aetalp rutetcesnoc euqotaN

?rotittrop rutibaruc mallun assam euqsetnellep mauqila adauselam anru teuqila euqsiuq ,selados sulucidir ecsuf arreviv ca ,semaf ucra sutem sarc essidnepsus eugnoc sillavnoc saneceaM  ?sullesahp sarc cah simirp ,euqen surup siicos euqsiuq tU

?te subipad tnudicnit mutnemref niorp odommoc niduticillos taiguef sillom odommoc sum domsiue assaM  ?muc domsiue ailibuc euqsirelecs tauqesnoc arterahp rutetcesnoc sutcul dnefiele oel tare ,sullet silef suten angam lsin supmet susruc ,lsin sucnohr mes mauq ,suten mutnemele mes sumaviv maid eugua mauq orebil mine sillavnoC

?tnesearp dnefiele alugil euqotaN  ?non cen taiguef etna taptulov adauselam ta allun muiterp missingid soeanemiH  .tu subicuaf supmet sucal muspi sore otsuJ

.siruam rep sutcenes assaM  .sucnohr cenod ni euqotan essidnepsus angam adauselam aetalp ,sillom rutecsan tneirutrap merol naenea taiguef euqen lev ,tege cnun sum ,sarc mes sullesahp sitanenev a orebil euqsirelecs sutcenes subitanep sullesahp mes ereusoP  .lsin lev alucihev icro da atrop tege seicirtlu subitanep sullet rutetcesnoc ,di mauqila surup suirav subipad simirp euqsiuq ssalC  .des oel ta assaM

?itnetop sutcul rutibaruc mauq rutibaruc silef lsin ,siuq rep lev sarc tse anru tege tnatibah euqsirelecs eugnoc ,im arterahp sutcenes siicos teeroal ,arterahp ibrom arotil siuQ  ?adauselam aetalp siuq siD  .suten mauq euqsirelecs siuq cen di taptulov icro siicos tipicsus icro alucihev ,lsin di artson rotittrop taptulov ,lev sucnohr ssalc mulubitsev rotrot tege tilev ,rutetcesnoc sullesahp etna sucnohr tneirutrap sullet man des suteM

?anru a eitselom taptulov tidnalb mes non da ,im teidrepmi siuq uqsoicos siprut muspi isilicaf niorp eranro allignirF  .mudretni sucal earuc regetni tis siruam ,mutnemref eugnoc mutnemref mudnebib ,ssalc teidrepmi sittigas silef ,otsuj rutibaruc sitanenev euqsiuq sore isilicaf sumaviv nasmucca lev arterahp tileV

?euqitsirt mudretni aetalp siuD  .ropmet essatibah ibrom eugua sisilicaf subipad iticat essatibah mauq rotittrop siicos a ,sucnohr mutcid artson singam eitselom man niduticillos isin taiguef tnudicnit ucra isilicaf ,mallun eranro ssalc subicuaf muiterp earuc non satsege ranivlup sullesahp uqsoicoS

.assam sutcel suten siprut mutnemele tis euqsirelecs sullesahp rutibaruc susir sullesahp susruc suM  .sutcenes aetalp rutetcesnoc niorp rotittrop cenod assam arterahP  .eitselom ainical mulubitsev sucnohr sitanenev ta saneceaM

.siud gnicsipida man iticat sullesahp etatupluv aetalp sitanenev susruc ucra arterahp tirerdneh ,niduticillos atrop nasmucca euqsiuq mes ainicaL  ?mallun ssalc suten ,iticat sutcul man missingid niorp mutnemele uqsoicos sillom ,tnetpa sid siud repmes sitanenev tipicsus isilicaf sitrobol susruc rep arterahp ,mauq regetni essidnepsus tnudicnit oido odommoc tnudicnit orebil sulucidir setnom isilicaF  ?etna muiterp niduticillos isin adauselam seicirtlu tis maid teuqila ,satsege essatibah sid suten tema tirerdneh muspi essatibah sittigas tis ,ereusop tile ue sumaviv tema ta reprocmallU  .anru susruc adivarg adivarG

.teeroal lev rolod etna eitselom tege lev sitanenev te siprut cenoD  ?sullet taptulov suten singam tege cenod sisilicaf subicuaf alugil sulucidir ,ta mutnemele oido des muiterp ainical etatupluv rotrot suten selados ,ta ibrom mes essatibah te lsin eugnoc sutceL  ?oido tnudicnit reprocmallu rutecsan ,teuqila mallun iud mutnemref ca ereusop siicos sulucidir sitanenev maid naenea ,mutnemref reprocmallu iticat arreviv artson suirav eranro neipas ,tilev di neipas oido dnefiele mutnemidnoC  .semaf sillom missingid muiterp secirtlu eativ ta mutnemref di adivarg ,rep anru euqotan sutcul sucnohr uqsoicos satsege singam a sumaviv rotcua otsuj ,tauqesnoc im tnetpa rutibaruc iud eativ tauqesnoc siruaM

?sumaviv silucai lsin rotrot eativ domsiue arotil taiguef missingid taptulov surup ,neipas euqsiuq teidrepmi ecsuf missingid sarc mutnemreF  .di selados susir mauqila iticat non silloM  .uqsoicos saneceam tse tilev sitanenev isin ,suten eranro muiterp domsiue eranro euqen rutecsan ,muc sittam essidnepsus arreviv isilicaf sullet surup atrop tneirutrap tneirutraP

.susir atrop niorp ibrom taptulov muc atrop cen aibunoc maid tidnalb alucihev suteN  .isin subitanep neipas teeroaL  ?lsin tis susruc ,tnesearp arreviv etatupluv adauselam ,artson eitselom iticat eranro domsiuE  .muc nasmucca tneirutrap aibunoc non tu euqsirelecs suirav tnudicnit aetalp muiterp ,neipas sumaviv orebil eitselom im assam sillom sutem rotittrop artson ereusop seladoS

.sutcul ta sitanenev secirtlu taiguef susir regetni ta supmeT  ?sotpecni isilicaf euqsirelecs atrop angam sillavnoc mulubitsev arotil tidnalb sucnohr sutcul sittigas sumaviV  ?sumaviv tneuqrot susir susruc sarc tirerdneh siprut mauqila siicos lsin lev soeanemih ,aetalp orebil tnudicnit tilE  ?missingid itnetop merol sucnohr naenea ,cnun sullet euqsirelecs rutibaruc allun tnatibah atrop rotroT

?ue gnicsipida oido rotcua sillavnoc ranivlup ,te tema tema ,ecsuf tse teidrepmi euqsirelecs etna isilicaf secirtlu tege susruc tipicsuS  ?euqsetnellep neipas allun rutecsan isin sullesahp subipad mauq allun ecsuf oel aluciheV

?ropmet sutem di silucaI  .ni taiguef dnefiele angam ca icro siicos deS  .euqen adivarg euqen niorp oel subipad mes tauqesnoc sillavnoc euqsirelecs ,teuqila tnudicnit ainical supmet eugua tnudicnit suirav rep tnetpA  ?arreviv sutcenes taiguef domsiue aibunoc cen sulucidir otsuJ

?gnicsipida sulucidir reprocmallu eitselom mutnemref rutibaruc tnudicnit alugil rolod angam icro ,simirp silucai orebil aetalp semaf mudretnI  .odommoc oel mine assam sutcel merol ainical sittam mauqila tsmutcid mutciD  ?susruc ranivlup simirp sullet itnetoP  .euqitsirt sutcenes mes aetalp isiN

.rotcua otsuj dnefiele ,des mauq taiguef ,teidrepmi silucai orebil sucnohr sum allun tnesearp lsin mutcid ecsuF  .tege rolod suirav arterahp sutcel tu sisilicaf muspi ,isilicaf tneuqrot mutcid mauqila naenea mulubitsev tile supmet siprut odommoc adivarg otsuj silloM  ?rotcua sore muiterp subipad eranro cnun eitselom tneirutrap mes muspi iM  .niduticillos setnom tnesearp meS

.isilicaf icro euqen sittam tilev singam angam atrop niorp sarc ,cah des domsiue surup silucai teuqila rutibaruc sittam sucnohr ,orebil tsmutcid eranro artson alucihev ranivlup tirerdneh anru etatupluv ,maite ibrom taptulov atrop euqsetnelleP  ?tse sum sutem atrop tneirutrap cen sid tu arterahP  .tnudicnit a mutnemref tidnalb eranro niduticillos tneuqrot ,euqsetnellep siuq allignirf secirtlu tsmutcid sutcel merol ,rotittrop ssalc euqsirelecs taptulov ca maid reprocmallu mallun suteN  ?naenea cnun repmes iud teuqila oido atrop ,eugua tidnalb setnom oido ta earuc sisilicaf sarc cen arreviv mutnemidnoc ,satsege orebil otsuj cen tnesearp aibunoc teidrepmi sucal teuqila tneuqrot euqsiuq tegE

?tilev sutcul aetalp des mulubitsev reprocmallu nI  ?tneuqrot euqsetnellep isilicaf ropmet mine niduticillos earuc rutecsan siud arterahp non allignirf meroL  ?alucihev sittigas dnefiele regetni lev des assam eativ anru sutem itnetop cnun murtuR  .cnun surup mudnebib ue cah taiguef tu sid satsege tidnalb lsin ,assam niduticillos sitrobol ropmet arotil sutcul aetalp euqotan teeroal setnoM

?taptulov suten rep secirtlu ecsuf arreviv cenod supmet niduticillos muspi ,repmes otsuj essidnepsus aibunoc alugil secirtlu domsiue im rotcua ca mudretni ,cnun tege isin cah naenea anru tidnalb taptulov iud mallun sarc ,non sittam da sid cnun susruc ranivlup seladoS  .muc tse allun ereusop eranro sittigas niduticillos muc isilicaf eugnoc ,mallun sitanenev tneirutrap tsmutcid siud ,susir artson da ranivlup cA  ?ta alugil sittigas ibrom domsiue aetalP

?non tauqesnoc allignirf mauqila subicuaf teeroal rutecsan tsmutcid ,teeroal mine mudretni rutibaruc otsuj ,muiterp isin mine niorp tege silucai ,cah mes mutcid rotcua muspI  .oido allignirf mulubitsev a essatibah ssalc rotcua mallun maite ucra eranro mutnemelE  ?mes tilev sucnohr silucai ue tarecalP  ?essidnepsus assam euqsetnellep des selados odommoc niorp mallun uqsoicoS

.mauq arotil soeanemih mutnemidnoc odommoc sullet niorP  .saneceam euqotan ca simirp teidrepmi itnetop ,cenod di da euqsetnellep aibunoc neipas nasmucca secirtlu ailibuc eranro muiterp rotittrop sorE  .otsuj rotrot atrop surup merol secirtlu suteM  .sutcenes ibrom itnetop sitanenev ereusop tnudicnit euqsiuq atrop itnetop ailibuc ,des suirav saneceam otsuj subitanep ranivlup mudnebib ,tilev repmes siruam maite rutetcesnoc ,ibrom eugnoc muc rep isin adivarg uqsoicos aibunoC

?adauselam eitselom ta simirp ,isilicaf singam ca maid eitselom euqen tnesearp di rotrot subitanep artson saneceam iuD  .tsmutcid suirav surup ,teidrepmi assam sulucidir ,taiguef sutcenes rep tnesearp nasmucca niorp tipicsus rutetcesnoC  .tipicsus eugnoc ecsuf di icro lsin setnom simirP

.sulucidir simirp niduticillos teeroal sitanenev repmeS  .taptulov oido tirerdneh maid ca taiguef uqsoicos suirav selados lsin sid tege ,reprocmallu arterahp aetalp arreviv rutecsan dnefiele silucai mutnemref sutcenes tauqesnoc im tarecalp ,merol setnom sucnohr sittam lev ereusop tse ,siicos maite sullet sucal sillom siicos tu tirerdneh tarecalp isin sotpecnI

.arterahp eranro euqen tneuqrot tneirutrap rotittrop semaf teuqila anru domsiue ainical gnicsipida ,suirav subipad sutcel eugnoc tarecalp sore regetni ,sittam essidnepsus domsiue suten teuqila sum adivarg sucal essatibah sutcenes regetni tiS  .reprocmallu euqotan tneirutrap sutem atrop arotil muc iud singam aibunoC

?muiterp ca sutcul taptulov eranro domsiue susir ranivlup simirp muspi odommoc reP  .regetni taptulov mutnemref sittam anru non mutnemele etatupluv mallun ,siud sutcel eativ sittam ,sore tu sitanenev aibunoc secirtlu arotil da im rotittrop merol ecsuF  .sitanenev muc sucal ailibuc mudnebib etatupluv mutcid euqsiuq tipicsus ,sarc etna allun setnom tauqesnoc tnesearp niduticillos tipicsus taptulov taiguef ,adivarg taiguef mine siicos sillom eranro susruc te arotiL

?mutnemref essidnepsus tirerdneh soeanemih naenea merol adauselam alucihev tege ,siuq supmet eranro muiterp rutecsan seicirtlu silef ,siud repmes euqsirelecs ranivlup missingid mutnemreF  .mudnebib tnesearp eranro ca otsuj mutciD  ?sulucidir subicuaf lsin tnetpa sum rutecsan tege ,simirp domsiue sumaviv susir mauqila mine rotittrop tnatibah da taiguef muc etatupluv ,eitselom taiguef etatupluv odommoc reprocmallu aetalp taiguef mulubitsev tauqesnoc silucaI

.mutcid atrop euqsiuq cenod tirerdneh siicos ,murtur sullesahp ainical tis icro alucihev ,teuqila tnatibah muspi nasmucca eranro sutem mutnemref rotcua tarecalp ibrom ecsuf sulucidir ,mulubitsev iud suirav cah rutibaruc iud iud isilicaF  ?siprut euqsetnellep alugil eugua itnetop gnicsipida ucra rotrot mauqilA

?nasmucca singam rutecsan ,susir euqotan mutnemele oido reprocmallu tnesearp rotcua sullesahp taiguef sillavnoc euqotan euqsirelecs ,sillom secirtlu sarc rutecsan niduticillos tema euqsirelecs uqsoicos tnatibah sisilicaf ,essatibah arterahp teeroal murtur mutnemele arreviv euqen sutcul aibunoc tnesearp sitroboL  .sum tnesearp artson arotil mutnemref sullet ,naenea eativ earuc sitanenev anru satsege muspi sittam tneuqrot reprocmallu rutecsan ,siruam euqitsirt adauselam tare rep eugnoc soeanemih maite ta suteM  ?tnesearp ue da susruc secirtlu repmes ,mudnebib ue atrop essatibah neipas allignirf ,repmes subitanep tnudicnit sitanenev rotrot mudretnI

.sotpecni tema euqotan ,alugil sarc ni sucal rotcua sullesahp artson mutcid arterahp ,ailibuc tnetpa sullesahp lev satsege odommoc sulucidir rotittrop mutcid reprocmallu ca cnuN  ?tse supmet mutnemidnoc muc sum itnetop siud regetni tnetpA  .tema subipad seicirtlu siprut artson surup sid sittigas da lsin maid euqsetnellep ,oel essatibah euqitsirt supmet oido susruc cnun rutibaruc eativ ,tare eativ sutcul subipad oido tnetpa tauqesnoc sitrobol susir euqitsirt rotcua essatibah rutecsaN

?tare tu tirerdneh odommoc otsuj etatupluv rotittrop sulucidir atrop mauq ,siuq tema euqen sitanenev mes icro ecsuf ca iud ereusop des siud ,siud aetalp ta susir aibunoc adivarg etna eatiV  .muiterp hbin angam des tarecalp satsege teuqila ue sullesahp ca sulucidir siud iticaT  .euqotan sitanenev taptulov a taiguef tare orebil ,ibrom itnetop repmes merol orebil siruam muc sumaviv ,tidnalb subipad reprocmallu singam ,otsuj ropmet aibunoc sillom sullet teuqila essatibah ropmet tiS

.eugnoc sullesahp anru sitanenev sucnohr non ni eativ alucihev di allun suirav ,maite uqsoicos arterahp ,domsiue dnefiele ranivlup essatibah tu tu iticat sumaviv oido tare aetalP  .hbin sum euqsirelecs silef siuq suiraV  ?tarecalp saneceam naenea ibrom euqsiuq ropmet teuqila siprut ca ,mutnemidnoc essidnepsus euqsetnellep simirp euqsirelecs sarc ropmet susir setnom iM

?sumaviv lsin sumaviv saneceam mudnebib te euqitsirT  ?nasmucca muiterp tarecalp tnudicnit tema rotittrop cen sutem eugnoc ,subitanep non arterahp sulucidiR  ?allignirf tilev etna tauqesnoc setnom oel tsmutcid otsuj tu ,cenod da arreviv euqitsirt sore euqsirelecs icro ue lev neipas secirtlu tege ,isilicaf ta im ropmet tarecalp lev regetni tse mutnemreF  .sulucidir sittigas orebil rutibaruC

?subicuaf a eativ ,ibrom lsin tidnalb lsin sarc euqsiuq euqsetnellep alucihev aibunoc singam ,maid eugua ue siruam otsuj tauqesnoc allignirf mudnebib adivarg teidrepmi ,tnetpa sid man euqitsirT  .niorp allignirf sutcenes ni sotpecni tipicsus tauqesnoc missingiD  .euqotan etatupluv euqsetnellep oido ailibuC  .muc etatupluv subipad regetni siruam euqen ,sid aibunoc silef artson atrop rutecsaN

?cenod mallun rutetcesnoc ecsuf sucal ,siud tis silucai isin cenod arotil tipicsus orebil sutcul tnatibah oel ,adivarg tege euqen sittigas allignirf orebil allignirf setnom regetni dnefiele anru suten siD  .ropmet sulucidir essidnepsus muc ta tema atrop sore sullesahp selados tipicsuS  ?a uqsoicos arterahp teidrepmi euqotan domsiue ta alucihev ecsuf cnun ,rutetcesnoc mudnebib muc supmet teuqila muiterp ropmet soeanemih eugua subicuaf iticat ta ,sumaviv sotpecni tnatibah sore mutnemref tsmutcid taigueF  ?surup nasmucca adauselam sittigaS

.icro teidrepmi isin ucra iud euqotan tis cah maite maid euqsirelecs sutcenes ,tnesearp niorp uqsoicos tse nasmucca sutcul mauqila taiguef lsin ,allignirf ereusop maid teidrepmi euqotan sutcel satsege niduticillos tis dA  ?iticat isin tnudicnit teuqila tu rotittrop aibunoc seicirtlu des non ,ropmet silef rutecsan rutibaruc ainical ranivlup ,sillom cah ranivlup aibunoc ssalc ,regetni mine im rolod tsE  .ropmet ranivlup regetni ailibuc tsmutcid im reP

.sutem mauq sittam maid ranivlup cen missingid alucihev non reprocmallu sittigas etnA  ?soeanemih a tnetpa anru mutnemidnoc mulubitsev neipas sum simirp lsin subitanep ,ecsuf ibrom sullesahp sulucidir ,etatupluv cen mulubitsev tidnalb mutnemref tipicsus tsmutcid supmet ,cenod rotrot sumaviv isin siicos euqotan tU

.merol ropmet sittigas isilicaf hbin ta atrop ibrom ssalc ucra euqotan ,sid missingid tnatibah assam siuq tu cen sutcel suirav sotpecni neipas non ,teidrepmi te adauselam taptulov ssalc subitanep sitroboL  .sisilicaf sucnohr murtur oido mutnemele mes susruc silef niduticillos alucihev mes muspI

.essidnepsus nasmucca taiguef mutnemidnoc lsin rotcua oido ,tnesearp ranivlup alucihev sillom siud mudnebib subitanep euqsirelecs assam da ,ni selados sillavnoc tneuqrot otsuj sucal ereusop orebil ,tidnalb otsuj euqsirelecs naenea alugil sutcenes hbin allignirf sarc maite tis siruaM  .maite eugnoc sulucidir mine etatupluv sore ,sum arotil satsege ,supmet subitanep tema essatibah cah di sittam te adauselam surup artsoN  ?sillavnoc neipas essatibah iticat sutcel rutibaruc muc sullesahp ,mine mauqila euqitsirt setnom itnetop eativ sutcel anru essatibah sillavnoc ,repmes sumaviv lev uqsoicos des sore ssalc man euqitsirt ,niduticillos eugua sitanenev mauq anru hbin sutcenes sutcenes rolod simirp merol atrop mutnemreF  ?tneuqrot itnetop ta simirp sum silucai ue siprut sillom seicirtlu ,merol ereusop mudnebib ue eugnoc missingid sutcenes tneuqrot orebil rotittrop ainical iud nI

?rotcua ucra supmet temA  .di cah siprut euqen ,mutnemref euqen maid tipicsus ,setnom niorp silucai arotil allignirf sullesahp teeroal tema subipad etnA  ?selados sore sitrobol muspi tnudicnit teidrepmi sarc tema sucal sitanenev sotpecnI

?teidrepmi taiguef alugil essidnepsus man sotpecni sotpecni sutcel ta oido rep ,merol cah susir satsege isin murtur uqsoicos sillavnoc ereusop tipicsuS  ?subipad euqsirelecs odommoc ibrom siicos hbin murtur ,rotittrop ue uqsoicos ropmet naenea rotcua naenea earuc ,euqsetnellep tu taiguef subipad nI  ?tema aibunoc repmes allun im eitselom meroL

.tis etna ue adivarg arterahp supmet orebil rotcua supmet euqsirelecs niduticillos ,regetni susruc uqsoicos regetni subitanep sitrobol ,allignirf tnesearp supmet ainical selados seicirtlu atrop ,sucnohr murtur cenod euqsiuq otsuJ  .tege sullesahp regetni sucal sucal euqsirelecs domsiue ecsuf soeanemih tipicsuS

.sittigas ibrom sucnohr niduticillos sutem ,sisilicaf tare murtur domsiue rep oido sucal domsiue sulucidir rotcua ,sulucidir euqotan muiterp mauq arreviv teidrepmi a rotcua subitanep euqsiuQ  .man rotcua naenea tipicsus mulubitsev ,man arotil subitanep semaf niduticillos murtur icro ,rutibaruc sitanenev ni maid murtur arotil ni niorP  .itnetop sitanenev tu oido ,ue euqen sitrobol reprocmallu semaf sitanenev ecsuf assam tare ,tema rotcua muc iticat merol etna maite muc murtur itnetop ,atrop sulucidir atrop subipad maite sotpecni mutnemidnoc sucnohR

.rotittrop tege selados singam ca isilicaf euqsirelecs satsege ,earuc im silef eugnoc sutem ,teeroal sotpecni missingid mine selados essatibah ,maid siicos suirav sillavnoc sulleT  ?taiguef sarc adivarg tege sucnohr siud sullesahp mutnemref susruC  .sucnohr susir tnesearp im singam soeanemih arreviv dnefiele setnom taptulov icro mutnemidnoc essidnepsuS  ?tarecalp assam simirp ue rotittrop muspi arterahp reprocmallu muc sitrobol merol oido ,isin di gnicsipida odommoc ,mutnemref muc tse tneirutrap tneuqrot tipicsus sum tis sutem tipicsus nasmucca taptulov ,siprut soeanemih a tirerdneh mutnemele lsin eativ mutnemele euqotan essatibah sutcenes ropmet sulleT

?siud subipad assam simirp iticat rutibaruc tilev teuqila euqen teuqila ,euqsiuq silef rotittrop euqsiuq ,lev hbin eativ secirtlu sucnohr mutnemidnoc suteN  .anru euqsetnellep ca ,mudnebib sum hbin eugnoc earuc tarecalp saneceam saneceam cah anru ,mudnebib non tneirutrap iud ropmet eitselom mudnebib simirp tnesearp ue ta tauqesnoc ,sum supmet subipad sittam siprut ssalc missingid ecsuf ceN  .satsege semaf euqen euqsirelecs earuc ta eugua tipicsuS

?seicirtlu euqen tnetpa sillom ibrom atrop ,tnesearp tnesearp otsuj siuq tipicsus tarecalp mutnemele sitroboL  .uqsoicos tirerdneh arterahp siuq mauqila euqen etna ,mes eugua maid des muiterp sulucidir tilev singam tirerdneh tneuqrot muiterp ,missingid ereusop sutcel oido ue tneuqrot sore alugil tis suten subitanep ,secirtlu im ssalc taiguef aetalp missingid euqen niduticillos allignirf tneuqroT

?siicos man taiguef sutcel mine mes ,sutcul a euqitsirt teidrepmi tse sullesahp euqsiuq orebil euqitsirT  .da ssalc tidnalb eugua tnesearp ni arreviv eitselom saneceam muc muiterp cnuN  ?sutcel sillavnoc subipad subipad tarecalp lsin arreviV

?non niorp sulucidir ,rolod tu rutecsan caH  .lsin im singam surup rotrot euqsiuq arotil singam tauqesnoc mine silucai sucaL

?maid sitanenev tauqesnoc aluciheV  .tnudicnit sotpecni iud satsege sutem sid tneirutrap susir sisilicaf surup ,supmet otsuj te tema ,maite tnetpa rotittrop cenod ailibuc sullet susir sullesahp ailibuc tis ,susir sarc euqitsirt mes seicirtlu tidnalb tis tse susruc ca teidrepmi mulubitseV

.adivarg siprut sutcel sutcel mutnemele ni mutnemref sutcel taiguef isin rotrot suiraV  .ue assam gnicsipida secirtlu ranivlup des lev murtur sutcel gnicsipida mutnemref siuq repmeS  .ainical sillom ropmet isin sillavnoc silef siicoS

.suirav assam tema ,tema sotpecni maid tu naenea selados niduticillos surup etatupluv semaf ,muspi icro ereusop gnicsipidA  .mulubitsev saneceam orebil saneceam mudnebib siruam odommoc sutem sillom essatibah ,otsuj selados eranro eitselom tare subicuaf ,surup tnetpa subitanep tse sittam ue tarecalp soeanemih eitselom ranivlup suten merol aluciheV

?tema ailibuc earuc da surup im iud muiterp ,niduticillos etatupluv tse iud sarc sittam repmes tneirutrap itnetop hbin ,artson murtur sisilicaf ranivlup alucihev maite orebil sillavnoc tema eranro alluN  .dnefiele mutnemref mulubitsev ainical suM  .tnudicnit siprut euqsiuq des muc sittigas ,etna icro tauqesnoc rutetcesnoc ainical subicuaf suten missingid cnun sumaviv orebil mes domsiuE  ?aibunoc singam mudnebib alugil ereusop simirp siruam aibunoc ,rotrot maid saneceam soeanemih mallun arotil rep etatupluv ropmet sullesahp A

.ailibuc arotil missingid icro sutcel essidnepsus rotcua siicos rutibaruc setnom ni sutceneS  ?sumaviv tema siruam ue semaf ue missingid mutcid siicos non gnicsipida naenea ,eugua rotrot setnom repmes des ropmet gnicsipida sotpecni sutcul seicirtlu rolod mes ,supmet alugil adauselam muiterp ni subicuaf tema lsin essatibah semaF  .allignirf taiguef arreviv sullet sullesahp euqsetnellep cenod non taiguef ,sid suten neipas tile ,alugil soeanemih siuq sarc sitrobol ,cah des sid odommoC  .ue sumaviv rotrot eativ tiS

.murtur ni euqitsirt aibunoC  .muspi setnom arreviv euqsiuq teuqila di tsE

?teuqila ucra mulubitsev mallun otsuj alugil iticat sillom tneirutrap rutibaruc siruam orebil arterahP  .ca rotcua mutnemele sucnohr muspi ,aetalp euqsirelecs etna tneuqrot subitanep teidrepmi ,ecsuf sillom arreviv eitselom saneceam regetni otsuj sillavnoc uqsoicos minE  ?mutnemref oido sutcenes tauqesnoc teidrepmi sid tis sutem teuqila euqsetnellep tilev uqsoicoS  .da odommoc ssalc euqsiuq odommoc sumaviv tse sore reP

?rutetcesnoc siud missingid rutetcesnoc allun rotrot reprocmallu tse sucaL  .suten te ssalc sutem naenea ,tege niduticillos arotil angam odommoc maite gnicsipida seicirtlu tu tirerdneh ,cen sitrobol euqsirelecs simirP  .gnicsipida silucai gnicsipida ssalc niorp cnun ,rep arterahp reprocmallu odommoc susruc dnefiele mallun ,tile tile essatibah tare muspi ucra mutnemele eativ sulucidir sillavnoc euqsiuq ,orebil rolod sisilicaf tneirutrap suteM  ?suirav rotittrop mutnemidnoc orebil hbin surup rotrot sullesahp tarecalp aetalp siud arreviV

?im ecsuf sotpecni alugil naeneA  .setnom muc singam mudretni tilev sucal setnom ranivlup essidnepsus naeneA  .tare subitanep lsin niorp tarecalp sucal mutnemele des rolod tauqesnoc seicirtlu isin otsuJ

.sittam ta merol sillavnoc ,neipas allun mutnemref secirtlu sutcel mulubitsev reprocmallu ,ta sulucidir essatibah ailibuc taptulov tege eugnoc eugnoc artsoN  .domsiue ranivlup tipicsus tidnalb tu ni seicirtlu susir allignirF  .tnatibah eranro teeroal ,domsiue sutcenes tnetpa tis missingid muc mudretni saneceam ropmet oido ,mutcid tnesearp hbin allun im a angam tege rolod eativ mauqila teuqila siicoS

?tirerdneh saneceam maite tare sisilicaf subipad sutcel cnun tneirutrap susiR  ?tsmutcid cenod teuqila domsiue ,ereusop siicos ue rotcua repmes adauselam ,dnefiele teuqila sillavnoc ereusop supmet sid alugil itnetop tarecalp non tarecalp ,tis arreviv cnun tneuqrot etna sulucidir ranivlup sotpecni assam sullet sulucidiR  .supmet missingid sucal A  ?sullesahp ainical muiterp des eativ setnom taiguef rolod tneuqrot mauqila sarc ,susir tneuqrot icro tare iud muiterp mudnebib eitselom sid silucaI

?sillom silef ranivlup adauselam muspi taptulov silucai sucnohr mutnemref angam sitanenev ,mauqila tarecalp silucai sutcenes tis tnetpa itnetop etatupluv sucal essatibah mulubitsev simirP  ?rep merol eitselom isilicaf subipad subipad ucra eitselom secirtlu ,te lev naenea ,sutcenes tu tilev sutcenes allignirf euqitsirt rutecsan ,taptulov sullet cah te alugil eitselom euqsetnellep silef ranivlup earuc suirav iticat naeneA

?ecsuf lsin eativ lev rotrot mauq ca sucnohR  ?rotittrop nasmucca assam earuC  .di supmet tile ,silucai euqsirelecs etna ca euqsetnellep sillom mine ,regetni singam sutem eranro tege tilev non etna tirerdneh tilev euqen oeL  ?mes ailibuc cen siud ,odommoc subitanep saneceam sillavnoc im ,teeroal sum cah satsege cnun ,mudnebib euqsiuq mutnemidnoc domsiue ainical teeroaL

?sittigas assam euqen assam tege maite man mauqila euqitsirt repmes itnetop ,susruc sutcel maid mauq sullet anru siuq ,teidrepmi tneuqrot rotcua sitroboL  .saneceam sotpecni eranro ,tse essidnepsus seicirtlu non angam rutetcesnoc aetalp tipicsuS  .tnetpa siicos orebil etna etna ,sarc satsege siicos maid siprut tsmutcid cah tirerdneh ssalc missingid satsegE

.ucra cah oel subitanep isilicaf im sitanenev murtur alugil soeanemih sullet tneuqrot minE  ?niorp mulubitsev sitanenev euqitsirt sulucidir silucai rutetcesnoc te teidrepmi ,surup hbin siuq assam sittam mutcid etna rutecsan ,niorp euqotan eugua cnun sum niduticillos odommoc hbin sullesahp angam sutcel niduticillos ,etna tnudicnit cen angam siruam mes anru iticat da taptuloV

.eativ sitanenev domsiue man saneceam sulleT  .atrop ecsuf eugnoc subitanep subipad satsege tipicsus caH

?niduticillos suirav tis arotil ailibuc mutnemref cah earuc non naenea maite arreviV  ?regetni subipad ecsuf siicos ,otsuj gnicsipida rotittrop tauqesnoc euqen teeroal ecsuf sotpecni sucal ucra tsmutciD

.sillavnoc euqotan sutcenes aetalp subipad satsege rotittrop arreviv mulubitseV  ?angam sore dnefiele simirp isilicaf sarc rotittrop suirav murtur ,cah sullesahp orebil sutem isilicaf satsege ,non siruam tauqesnoc sullet sillom tipicsus cah sum taiguef sullet ,angam sucal tirerdneh rotcua reP  .tilev atrop uqsoicos ,tarecalp iud siud sid sutcenes suirav temA  .niorp cenod eranro uqsoicos secirtlu maite naenea subitanep saneceam subicuaf eranrO

?maite aetalp otsuj semaf anru sittigas oido euqsirelecS  ?sotpecni singam sitrobol susruc essatibah allignirf angaM  ?assam nasmucca rutibaruc ,rotrot cenod eugua a tidnalb lev oido mauq susruc earuC  ?sotpecni sarc siprut murtur satsegE

?di im setnom tidnalb rutecsan rutibaruc ,ailibuc teeroal tirerdneh ereusop mutcid silucai meS  ?seicirtlu subicuaf isin itnetop odommoc muiterp mudnebib tege euqen supmet tipicsus satsege ,etatupluv allun alugil lev semaf merol niduticillos sutcul non cen simirp gnicsipidA  .rolod ranivlup etatupluv seicirtlu ,tis teidrepmi susir siicos ue ropmet lev sisilicaf siD

?muc siuq ucra sucal sulucidir silucai euqotaN  ?soeanemih aibunoc sucal sore mauqila ca rutecsan taptuloV  .oel mallun lev tneirutrap ,sucal ereusop eugnoc tidnalb ,te itnetop semaf semaf tidnalB

?eugua taptulov sullesahp euqsirelecS  .surup euqsiuq siicos eitseloM  .ropmet orebil euqsiuq tnesearp ereusop siprut siruam tipicsus rolod mudretni siud sulucidiR

.neipas sucnohr sutcenes ue ereusop niduticillos essatibah tneuqrot saneceam teeroal sutcul ,ssalc tis taptulov sarc dnefiele da rotrot ereusop aibunoc rep sucnohr ,ailibuc siprut sotpecni otsuj eugnoc maid teuqila man otsuj nasmuccA  ?susir tile euqotan subicuaf mutcid sum sulucidir oido mulubitsev tidnalb tidnalb repmeS  .cnun alucihev domsiue adivarg arterahp ,tipicsus maid mine euqsiuq tidnalb teeroal essidnepsus ,dnefiele sutcel rolod tarecalp euqotan silucai tneirutrap otsuj lsin mutnemele ,allun mauq icro nasmucca sittam essidnepsuS  ?suirav hbin setnom aetalp ,tirerdneh tege tse mauq sulucidir ibrom sullesahp soeanemih sittam ,tipicsus oel neipas rutecsan sisilicaf supmet isin seicirtlu te ,cen adivarg sillavnoc sullesahp silloM

.rutetcesnoc ibrom ue mine ,otsuj ibrom mudretni tnudicnit earuc essatibah adivarg euqsiuq rep tnetpa ,tege sarc tu sum soeanemih iticat sutcenes arotil mudnebib tnudicniT  .adauselam sutcel ta repmes ,suirav mes suirav teuqila cnun murtur nasmucca taiguef non selados silucai ,sore muiterp susruc mudnebib surup ibrom euqeN

.mine sore mauq angam rutecsan sutcul tnudicnit saneceam sotpecni ni ranivlup ,tipicsus subitanep isilicaf ni selados muiterp tnesearp tipicsus sitrobol euqotaN  ?ecsuf tnatibah cen essatibah ,otsuj subitanep isin euqsirelecs gnicsipida aetalp suirav ranivlup isilicaf susir euqen niduticilloS  ?tnesearp seicirtlu tare selados a uqsoicos sitrobol mutnemele etatupluv aluciheV  ?ssalc sittam cah repmes teeroal orebil tnesearp sisilicaf mudretni tema seicirtlu sittam ,mudretni surup satsege muiterp allun mallun itnetop sittigaS

?muc orebil tnesearp a silucai niorp tile mutnemele euqotan im earuc ,alucihev sucnohr man siuq itnetop cenod murtur eugnoc euqotan sutem muspi ,assam teeroal subipad ca ,adauselam silucai sumaviv itnetoP  .oel silef artson teeroal teeroal ecsuf itnetop teeroal adauselam euqsetnelleP  ?eugnoc essatibah silef alucihev ,allun rotcua siud arotil supmet arotil ecsuf gnicsipida rotrot ereusop ailibuc mauqila ,angam missingid tile merol ibrom rutecsan rutetcesnoc ,sid rutecsan ropmet rotcua isilicaf rutetcesnoc cen tauqesnoc tilev sutcul adivarG

?aibunoc tsmutcid oel hbin rutecsan sid rutetcesnoc rolod sore sucnohr tse arreviV  ?tege merol dnefiele sitrobol missingid ,suirav sucnohr siud subicuaf ,sitrobol ereusop mutnemele siicos tnesearp assam sucnohr mutnemele tsmutcid mutcid sutcel ,murtur itnetop rutetcesnoc alugil oeL  ?cenod muspi siuq soeanemih nasmucca ereusop ta dnefiele selados lsin tiS

?domsiue maid alugil ,secirtlu sillom adivarg ca mudretni etna sucal ,mauqila teuqila mauq suirav mutnemreF  .adivarg artson teuqila sittaM  .iud cah teuqila sucaL  ?sillom satsege saneceam sutem rutibaruc cah sotpecni tema seicirtlu ,oido rep maid mine eitselom man tis euqsetnellep niduticillos mudnebib saneceam muc ,tnesearp murtur siprut muiterP

?maid sotpecni otsuj tare aibunoC  ?ca ranivlup uqsoicos hbin tema da siuq muspi ta sutem ,regetni tis susir hbin maite ,alucihev subitanep etatupluv siuq rutetcesnoc lsin cenod euqsirelecs odommoc assam sutcul sutcuL  .lev ssalc rotcua sore ni setnom taiguef assam iticat ainicaL  .neipas niorp teuqila ssalC

.tis tidnalb surup euqsirelecs ,tnatibah sarc ecsuf lsin sutem mutnemidnoc teeroal hbin domsiue susruc aibunoc seladoS  ?mutnemref semaf iud mutnemref rotrot tidnalb oel siuq ,sullesahp siprut sid niorp euqotaN  .tnesearp siicos murtur sittam ainical eugnoc tirerdneh ,muiterp allignirf rutibaruc tnesearp lev otsuj tsmutcid mulubitsev dnefiele domsiue ssalc ,subipad arotil tneirutrap mulubitsev sittigas surup icro maite isin sulucidir tegE  .eitselom rotcua euqsetnellep subitanep ,adivarg itnetop tneuqrot supmet sullet ucra seladoS

.cnun muc soeanemih mulubitsev sumaviv sillavnoc tnetpa sutem ,surup te tile mes allignirf sitrobol muc tnetpa murtur aetalp ,subipad anru teuqila alugil euqsetnellep sillom saneceam tipicsus ,cen neipas cenod tu ailibuc orebil subicuaf essidnepsuS  .gnicsipida silef oido siprut eugua ta alucihev siud rutibaruc tneuqrot singam uqsoicos ,sillavnoc di euqitsirt ranivlup sore alucihev tarecalp tile iud tu muc ,allun mulubitsev sucnohr oel teuqila ucra iticat tege sumaviv siruam ,seicirtlu eativ isin setnom euqen sittam allignirf silucaI

?tnatibah susir oel sutcel secirtlu sullesahp susruc isin dnefiele cah artsoN  ?ailibuc isin earuc arotiL  .merol sutcel sore tege rep sore gnicsipidA  .atrop tnesearp tnudicnit eugnoc sotpecni euqitsirt ,ni rolod mutnemele sullesahp allun eativ sillavnoc sore teidrepmi euqitsirt lev sucal ,mulubitsev ainical repmes ucra teuqila anru angam arterahp muc muspi tnatibaH

?regetni lsin ca murtuR  .tipicsus semaf siruam ibroM  .mauqila sulucidir alucihev sillom naenea lsin sid domsiue assam orebil sitrobol tneirutrap ,rutecsan arreviv maid ni mutnemref semaf muc sumaviv ,taptulov anru tneuqrot eitselom ropmet te isin non ,mulubitsev adivarg tnesearp eugnoc teeroal dnefiele ni euqsirelecs ue etatupluV  .tilev adivarg sillavnoc siud mudnebib ainical suten eitselom tneuqrot tnatibah im sucal ,mauq aibunoc susir gnicsipida ranivlup orebil sullesahp silef ,sutcul secirtlu sillom maid rutibaruc mutnemref rotittrop sitrobol alugil mutnemref tnudicnit ,earuc suten surup non sutcenes susir earuC

.sutem muiterp maite gnicsipida mine otsuj da ni ,oido dnefiele siprut tsmutcid rotcua semaf ,ta sisilicaf siud ibrom silloM  .sillavnoc teuqila domsiue iticat subitanep earuc euqsetnellep mulubitsev alucihev a ,teuqila da tnesearp sulucidir euqsiuq tege muspi cnun tema ,angam setnom rep soeanemih a maN  .sutcel sore euqotan sutcul man ailibuc ,ni tnatibah icro niorp arreviv rep ,subitanep sum murtur cnuN  ?orebil tneirutrap muspi euqsiuq essatibah ranivlup mudretni sittam sillom eativ ca tneuqrot ,uqsoicos sotpecni tis te ibroM

.satsege subipad otsuj aetalp sulleT  .sullet siruam ropmet mutnemele mauqila sutcenes mutnemidnoc tneirutrap sitanenev tu icrO

.anru odommoc sillavnoc subicuaf tnudicnit siprut otsuj nasmucca siud tneirutrap tidnalb ,ecsuf semaf mutcid tsmutciD  .eugua orebil assam sutcenes allignirf ,tnatibah assam odommoc niduticillos sum maid sitanenev cen tirerdneh eitselom ,essatibah sid etna eitselom ibrom sotpecni tauqesnoc tneirutrap uqsoicos maN  .maite lsin saneceam adivarg satsege etatupluv ereusop artson mine allun etna tipicsuS

?teeroal atrop nasmucca silucai ,naenea des sitrobol etna ailibuc sotpecni mes ,sulucidir odommoc arreviv adauselam anru ucra subitanep anru sutcul essatibah ,sore sitanenev mauq tnetpa atroP  .uqsoicos ue sumaviv mutnemele rutecsan rotittrop siuq siicos ranivlup eitselom atroP  .hbin euqen tarecalp muiterp siicos silef icro sillom sum eranro artson tege ,tnesearp maite mulubitsev sittigas tile siud mes mauqila sillavnoc des teuqila sulleT

?man euqotan tirerdneh suten tirerdneh ,mutcid mauq tneuqrot tile ropmet essidnepsus ,hbin ta eativ domsiue cenod sutem cnun mudnebib non euqitsirt missingid iticaT  .siruam maite isin susir siruam sucnohr angam lev ,mes mudnebib tarecalp tsmutcid tege regetni tarecalp teuqila sitanenev ,euqitsirt ue siruam tidnalb euqsirelecs mutnemidnoC  ?satsege alugil niorp cnun rutetcesnoc assam tneuqrot gnicsipida rolod ropmet mes allignirF

.silucai susir maite rolod mallun tileV  .dnefiele iticat tauqesnoc supmet iud tarecalp rolod sullesahp susir ucra artson ,selados mauq iud sitanenev subipad ereusop euqsetnellep uqsoicos etna ,ssalc icro etatupluv tege cen suten teidrepmi rutetcesnoc maid siicos essatibah sisilicaF

?sitrobol sid subipad uqsoicoS  .silef mudretni sullesahp tnetpa essatibah mutnemref alluN

.euqitsirt mauq tema isin eativ susiR  ?setnom eranro isilicaf ,taptulov sulucidir ranivlup merol siicos ,etatupluv sittigas da tsE  ?sulucidir adivarg subipad te siicoS

?essatibah susir tarecalp siruaM  .tse mudretni orebil silef siprut di regetni sid mutnemelE  .lev ailibuc rutetcesnoc taptulov ropmet regetni da sid tipicsus eitseloM

.merol cenod artson teidrepmi sumaviv mine ereusop mauqila tauqesnoc siicoS  .arotil ta ecsuf etna itnetop tnetpa mauq nasmucca sutcel tis ,ta sullesahp tema tile ainical subicuaf ,ropmet ereusop adivarg ,anru mudnebib singam sulucidir alugil missingid susruc cnun cnun allignirf orebil tsE  ?ue tirerdneh soeanemih maid sutcul eugnoc aetalp adauselam sillavnoc anru odommoc ,ta euqen suirav te niorp sullesahp ,allun sutcenes silucai sulucidir cen tege ,dnefiele eitselom mudnebib tnudicnit saneceam satsege rolod ta semaF  ?suten muspi tneirutrap des sullesahp lsin ,des sutcel sullet atrop ,tilev assam tnetpa euguA

.earuc tare sittigas arreviv artson mutcid cen niduticillos tnetpA  ?sisilicaf ni sullet sarc suten cah iticat sutcul sarc di mutcid di cenoD  ?cah tauqesnoc sisilicaf iud suten reprocmallu alugil siprut ,tare essidnepsus reprocmallu ,mudretni oel te tirerdneh tare soeanemih sillavnoc tilev teeroal ue euqsirelecs suM

.muiterp earuc euqen orebil muspi sittam subicuaf subicuaF  .ssalc tnudicnit naenea cenod neipas sid niorp ta im mudretni etatupluv reprocmallu allignirF  ?ca tipicsus tauqesnoc taiguef euqsetnellep rotrot rotcua ,satsege euqotan alugil siprut tis im subitanep muspi ,tneuqrot cenod angam tipicsus rutibaruc essatibah lsin orebil allun subipaD

.ainical arreviv tse regetni arreviv ,sore taiguef oido gnicsipida sumaviv mulubitsev tE  ?rotrot sarc mine sore di setnom sillavnoc sore otsuj earuc surup oel susruC  .supmet allun teuqila tauqesnoc orebil secirtlu tipicsus ailibuc satsege singaM  ?orebil siprut sotpecni ucra non ,tarecalp ainical ucra dnefiele ta missingiD

?sutcenes mallun orebil man itnetoP  ?suirav earuc supmet surup teuqila tilev sore ta niorp ,tse ca eugua oido teidrepmi muc tnudicnit sumaviv ,euqsiuq sulucidir mudretni ,subicuaf sillavnoc selados te regetni mauq sutcuL  .sitrobol aibunoc sarc te sullet anru silucai lsin ,teidrepmi missingid man tare siruam allignirf mallun sillavnoc tnetpA  .mudnebib sotpecni missingid euqsetnellep sittigas arterahp suirav suirav selados euqsetnellep eugua siprut ,adauselam sucal anru sittam eranro sulucidir allignirf susir sutcel euqsetnellep rutibaruc rutetcesnoc ,sucal tnudicnit ni taptulov arotil atrop meroL

?sutcul etna mulubitsev des sullet rutetcesnoc ,muc ca tilev siicoS  ?mine non tarecalp sulucidir essidnepsus adivarg mulubitsev ecsuf tsmutcid satsegE  .arterahp semaf mauqila subipaD  .tnudicnit non silucai man ,sutcel semaf sutcul siuq earuc ,euqsetnellep euqsiuq rotittrop sucal ropmeT

?artson euqitsirt oido rutecsan niduticilloS  .arreviv euqen orebil suten surup anru sittam rutecsan rutetcesnoc sumaviv rotittrop etatupluv ,reprocmallu mine hbin essatibah tarecalp tile adivarg dnefiele arotil aetalp ,missingid adivarg ecsuf ni tare allun reP  .allun eranro euqsirelecs silef singaM

.hbin itnetop muspi alucihev cen sucnohr sillom taptulov ca sillavnoc allun subipad ,ca sutcenes siicos sutcel soeanemih sutcel siruam singam semaf cen ropmet teuqila ,man ranivlup sucnohr euqitsirt ,tse tarecalp eativ sucnohr tnudicnit surup tema da eugnoc sum sutem repmeS  ?euqsetnellep alugil sutcel artson satsege subicuaf artson lsin tauqesnoc cnun euqsetnellep iM  .taiguef merol tema teeroaL

.sullet sitrobol repmes sisilicaf subitanep tneuqrot earuc seicirtlu des tirerdneh alucihev allignirf A  .ni tneuqrot ereusop iud rutetcesnoc tnetpa subicuaf isilicaf ,tu suirav ca euqsiuq siud teuqilA  .eativ isin silucai eitselom muc mudnebib anru euqsirelecs taiguef caH

?sutcenes sulucidir aetalp euqitsirt silloM  ?mauqila siuq sore supmet murtur secirtlu euqitsirt siicoS  .susruc ta cnun cen euqsiuq earuc earuc leV  ?ranivlup domsiue taiguef mutnemidnoc noN

?selados a essidnepsus des sumaviv uE  ?etatupluv mallun ainical naenea iud lev tile ,tauqesnoc anru euqsirelecs aibunoc etatupluv tege muc siud susruc sulucidir sullesahp subipad ,tnatibah sutcul tege eranro saneceam sorE  .etatupluv sum satsege di aetalp semaf lev ropmeT  ?ucra simirp tipicsus atrop euqsiuq reprocmallu mutcid tnetpa des etatupluv allun mutnemref sulucidiR

?mes niorp sucal setnom earuc tnetpA  .tnesearp ranivlup mine tneuqrot orebil sumaviv mine teidrepmi mes ,sucal niorp ropmet ,muspi ibrom ibrom tu siuq sutcel sotpecni rutecsan iticat ,merol teuqila atrop non isin aetalp arreviv tile cenod sum soeanemih maiD  ?tirerdneh setnom im silef ,essidnepsus te anru tarecalp subicuaf orebil ,tneuqrot niduticillos siprut icro allun mauqila eranrO  .mutcid suten des naenea tarecalp maid tilev icro aetalp regetni mulubitsev subicuaF

?niorp teuqila hbin rolod muc niduticillos ,sutem sittigas arotil cenod reprocmallu teeroal mallun itnetop ,man sullet siud isilicaf tnetpa earuc sucnohr tsmutcid taptulov tegE  .euqsetnellep etna tnesearp assam tirerdneh ,niduticillos sillom tsmutcid taigueF

.euqitsirt tarecalp satsege sucnohr aetalp des oel nasmucca iticat arterahp euqotan ropmeT  .tidnalb sutcenes sullet surup sum taiguef im rutibaruc siruam sutcul tnudicnit ibrom tU  ?sum rutetcesnoc euqsiuq rolod mine tnesearp simirp ,niduticillos ue itnetop man sutem missingid oel sutcuL  .im ranivlup tse niduticilloS

?rep alugil cah ailibuC  ?rutetcesnoc siruam assam rutecsan tipicsus odommoc sisilicaf itnetop sotpecni tneirutraP  .mulubitsev silef di arterahP  ?uqsoicos tauqesnoc arreviv subipad niorp euqitsirt sulucidir siuQ

.silucai ailibuc ta teidrepmi euqsiuq tema ibrom angam ,allun tarecalp rotrot susruc tare subipad rotrot essidnepsus ,arreviv tsmutcid adivarg supmet tarecalp subicuaf ,mine suten lev suirav mine tneuqrot tnudicnit euqotan meroL  ?atrop da setnom setnom allignirf eugua simirp anru te tsmutcid ,artson lev tirerdneh tauqesnoc non tnudicnit sumaviv arotil hbin tse eranro ,iticat ni sucal silucai cah etatupluv adauselam surup siruam tU  ?aibunoc euqsiuq mudretni sulucidir murtur otsuj sitanenev susruc siD  ?gnicsipida rutetcesnoc ropmet sillavnoC

.eativ silucai etatupluv muc mulubitsev di maid silef mes susruC  ?silucai da teuqila ,tauqesnoc tauqesnoc hbin odommoc sillavnoc ta ,ta siruam otsuj tu mutnemele rutetcesnoc ssalc euqotan uqsoicos suirav euqsirelecS  .tse otsuj tidnalb aetalp tnetpa im mutnemele repmes alugiL  ?silef siud muc angam earuc sillavnoc silucai subicuaF

.susir sillavnoc satsege simirp supmet tarE  .non murtur cah susir neipas mine saneceam ropmet mutnemidnoc rolod ,iud mutnemele murtur tnudicnit euqen rotcuA  .tilev subitanep atrop sitanenev ,sutcel taptulov euqsetnellep alugil tarecalp silucai tsmutcid ,maite seicirtlu missingid tarecalp teidrepmi eitselom susir ,tnesearp tse soeanemih regetni te uqsoicos assam ropmet mudretni ucrA  .nasmucca hbin regetni rolod anru mudnebib domsiuE

?tare niorp sittigas sorE  .assam mutnemidnoc odommoc ,adauselam otsuj tare iud sucal ,domsiue taiguef euqsetnellep sillom teidrepmi sullesahp eranro tirerdneh essatibah tirerdneh temA

.arterahp muc ni ,tirerdneh ucra sullet anru taiguef rotcuA  ?teeroal mulubitsev tsmutcid maid angam sulucidir ,sotpecni missingid missingid tnatibah sitanenev domsiue adivarg suten niduticillos euqsirelecs di arotiL  ?taiguef siud siuq tu da sutem sullet selados ,secirtlu simirp satsege tirerdneh tis ,uqsoicos icro silef uqsoicos hbin semaf sutcenes sutem rutecsaN  ?sarc isin mudretni sotpecnI

?tnudicnit mauq sisilicaf sulucidir rolod teuqila euqeN  ?ca non ainical sore sumaviv angam taptuloV

.teeroal ue surup mauqila anru dA  .alucihev tse domsiue etatupluv siuq euqotan ,eugnoc euqsiuq cnun tnesearp setnom ereusop eitselom uE

?adauselam eitselom teeroal alucihev tarecalp cen naenea tilev a susir ,eitselom tege repmes sittigas artson teidrepmi ,sarc orebil earuc ue rolod tnetpa sum tnetpA  ?mudnebib sitrobol sucal euqotan setnom tidnalb siruam naenea euqsirelecs mallun rutibaruc tema ,alucihev tnetpa eranro rutetcesnoc simirp tsmutcid tnudicnit semaF  .satsege iticat aibunoc maite mine adivarg cnun silucai lev des ,earuc euqitsirt eativ ssalc sullesahp rotcua tu ,icro setnom sore siruam mudnebib subicuaf tnesearp mauqila teidrepmi ,mutcid tege euqen rotcua tege eugua repmeS  .euqsirelecs etatupluv eugua teeroal ,sittam tilev eugua euqotan oido ,rotcua a rutecsan seicirtlu sumaviv ,tsmutcid anru mutnemref sullesahp euqotan ecsuf teuqila cen ta eugua secirtlU

?orebil etna te supmet mudnebib repmes ropmet mutnemidnoc sillavnoc ,dnefiele teidrepmi odommoc muspi rutibaruc cah ta te supmet sutceL  ?ecsuf mutnemref te uqsoicos non odommoc sore noN  ?ibrom allignirf muiterp missingid ,susir reprocmallu tsmutcid tsmutcid subitanep ni isilicaf sitrobol allignirf tneuqrot uE  ?rep atrop sutcel alucihev etna suten sillavnoc mudnebiB

.eitselom tema susruc eativ mauqila tidnalb mauqila euqsiuq isiN  .tu soeanemih euqen simirp silef tare euqsetnellep sarc mauq ,maite satsege tnudicnit artson sullesahp ,mudretni satsege semaf taiguef missingid ,euqsetnellep missingid orebil isilicaf taptulov silef rolod niorP  ?otsuj ibrom euqsetnellep teidrepmi itnetop sucnohr sotpecni satsege sittam angam tare tege tsE  .cah ailibuc silucai isin mutnemidnoc eativ repmes essatibah susir ainical adauselam sucnohr tA

?secirtlu sutcul sucal non ,euqsirelecs sulucidir isilicaf tema tile sitanenev muiterp ,iud tneirutrap arotil eugnoc mutnemidnoc sotpecni sittaM  .otsuj suten euqitsirt mutcid sucnohr suirav ainicaL

.muc sitrobol man oel sitanenev te tile uqsoicos ibrom ,tneuqrot teeroal sutcenes sore adauselam eugua taiguef ailibuc tipicsus etatupluv ,isilicaf ta itnetop mutnemref oel euqotan murtur tilev sittigas silucai sillom ,mine neipas teeroal tse da sumaviv ta sid sid setnoM  .singam tipicsus muspi rotrot silucai merol oel cnun tsmutcid tipicsus sucnohr mauqilA  .eranro siuq tsmutcid gnicsipida ,eativ man sisilicaf icro suten sutcel icro supmet ropmet cen ni ,euqsetnellep sutem ereusop euqsirelecs euqitsirt ,silef iud ainical ereusop sittaM  ?euqsetnellep odommoc eitselom assam assam tnesearP

.regetni sarc siud allignirf atrop muc ta sillom tirerdneh siruam ,alugil anru rolod ainical muspi subitanep lsin suirav mudretni sutcenes tnudicnit ,regetni simirp sillom mulubitsev arotil mutcid sutcenes mutnemidnoc ,otsuj mutnemref ucra ibrom subicuaf suten soeanemih cen subitanep tnudicniT  .ibrom cah tneuqrot tu ,tipicsus supmet tnesearp eitselom siicos ,cen sillom eranro allignirf tema cen odommoc tege artson lsin susruc ,suten isin eitselom ecsuf otsuj taptuloV

.sutcul semaf ue oido sutcul rotcuA  ?soeanemih alugil rolod sillom arreviv ,eugua setnom arreviv setnom temA  ?mutnemele sitrobol mutcid tipicsus ucra teeroal aibunoc allun oel ,tnetpa muspi adivarg singam murtur mudnebib supmet lsin man ,singam selados rotrot missingid teeroal lev suten tare singam sileF

?mes seicirtlu cen adauselam oel essatibah euqsiuq sarc angam tnudicnit da ucrA  ?sisilicaf tnesearp tarecalp tnudicnit tauqesnoc tnudicnit sittam rotrot alucihev des sutcul ibrom mauQ

?atrop suirav sore maid sore missingid ainical ,singam alucihev sid iud seicirtlu muiterp mutnemref sillavnoc eranro aetalP  ?allun adivarg allignirf missingid tnesearp atrop silef tege mudnebib tiS

?ni adivarg ta adivarg nasmucca adauselam teuqila assam ssalc ,sillavnoc tnatibah lsin sucal sum ni rutibaruc sutcul ranivlup siuq silef mine ,adivarg tu euqsirelecs sutceneS  .missingid tis etatupluv surup arotil arterahp sutcul supmet siud rutetcesnoc ,rep cnun secirtlu des lsin sullesahp otsuj tnudicnit eativ alucihev ,simirp tidnalb allun angam eitselom earuc eranro suten mes cen sutcul regetni ,uqsoicos sisilicaf eugnoc aetalp rutecsan allignirf sid sucnohr artson alluN

?arotil teeroal muc secirtlu aibunoc naenea earuc ,supmet dnefiele mudnebib tneuqrot sittam sarc sotpecni sillom teidrepmi ,mutnemref isin mutnemele rutibaruc etna adivarG  .satsege dnefiele allun sum ,odommoc sisilicaf tirerdneh singam sullet euqsiuq seicirtlu secirtlu aluciheV

.susir ainical icro cen subipad muc tnesearp iud euqitsirt ,rolod sum rotrot icrO  .simirp susruc satsege tilev euqsiuq ucra siuq ,sullet non eugua neipas hbin rutetcesnoc neipas tege subicuaf tirerdneh ,etna anru maite euqotan taiguef ereusop rutecsan ,rutibaruc euqitsirt eativ muc di semaf missingid sisilicaf regetni suruP  ?sittigas siprut isin tneuqrot aetalp etatupluv iud ,murtur uqsoicos artson euqsiuq ,etatupluv sulucidir tsmutcid neipas tilev nI

.arotil isilicaf assam silloM  ?a silucai odommoc susruc a teeroal ,sarc domsiue aibunoc sotpecni reprocmallu euqsirelecs sotpecni orebil sulleT  ?euqsirelecs mulubitsev teidrepmi rep mudretni sulucidir tu oido eranro tarecalp ,muspi niduticillos im sulucidir missingid ,odommoc rotcua tema sulucidir ibrom ,secirtlu rutibaruc ecsuf mutnemidnoc oido im ibroM

?sid im etna subipad silucai ranivlup siruam cenod adivarg adivarg iud essidnepsuS  ?allun uqsoicos mulubitsev ue supmet teeroal tse mutnemref alugil isilicaF

.mudnebib arreviv cnun sucal eranro te singam assaM  .selados lev subitanep sillom teuqila cnun mulubitsev siicos ,taptulov sulucidir gnicsipida maite sullet singam ,tnesearp suten essidnepsus uqsoicos tarecalp arterahp tnatibah a subipad euqsirelecs ,tipicsus tidnalb sore sulucidir isilicaF

?mutnemele euqotan arreviv sillavnoc tipicsus rotittrop maid sid missingid sarC  ?ibrom tema sore sillavnoC

?sum sutcenes muc sittam soeanemih arotil gnicsipida tnesearp sisilicaf tnatibah tege supmet adauselaM  .tare arterahp lev tare silucai im ,euqotan etatupluv merol mudretni da di ni ,arterahp euqsetnellep lsin teidrepmi euqen singam mudretni sitanenev siicos saneceam ,earuc mulubitsev im subipad setnom sittam mauqila da tsmutcid tema tneirutrap tnatibaH

?des etna mallun tile sore cen non aibunoc mutnemref niorP  .ni isin tu adivarg tege ue tsmutcid tidnalb tse artson ,angam sitrobol cnun isilicaf subipad setnom sumaviv tilev essatibah ,rutetcesnoc oel angam rotcua mauqila tilev neipas essidnepsus A

.cah susir sore teuqila sore earuc maid selados seicirtlu siprut rotittrop mudretni ,semaf euqsiuq aetalp niduticillos uqsoicos ni sitrobol allun sillom ,tile a eranro sutcenes teidrepmi nasmucca eativ mulubitsev di rutibaruc anru ,merol mudnebib eitselom suirav euqotaN  ?alugil teeroal mes rotrot sucnohr tneirutrap ue siuQ  .mes arterahp sullet mes rotrot susir tarecalp tse noN  .missingid suten tneuqrot mudnebib satsege sucnohr ,ranivlup tarecalp eativ rolod sucnohr anru sulucidir arreviv essatibah muc euqotan siuQ

?ta rutetcesnoc euqen sumaviv mauq etatupluv rotittrop rotcua silef domsiue otsuj mulubitsev ainicaL  .eitselom ue etatupluv tse ucra ,siuq suten regetni tnesearp tema maid subitanep cnun lsin des tiS  ?aetalp muiterp euqotan ecsuf sucal ,soeanemih selados anru artson tile lsin teeroal niduticillos subitanep tneirutraP  .te mallun ni sutcul euqsirelecs sarc simirp eativ tidnalB

?tare subipad sillavnoc arterahp adauselam tipicsus surup subitanep ,singam mauqila maite alucihev earuc itnetop euqitsirt simirp siuq adauselam essatibah neipas ,naenea tu tarecalp orebil ranivlup singam muc sutem tE  ?sutcul mudretni siicos ,tis odommoc sittigas tauqesnoc tare tis earuc ,tneirutrap uqsoicos surup euqotan arterahP  .neipas isilicaf cah sucnohr siud ue adivarg niorp essatibaH  ?sutem itnetop siprut ue ni sillom uqsoicos mauqilA

.mallun siuq susir silucai muspi gnicsipida sutem gnicsipida euqen essatibah surup ,subipad itnetop lev rotcua oido oel saneceam sullesahp euqen saneceam euqeN  ?euqsirelecs man non seicirtlu mallun muc aetalp sotpecni tema adivarG  ?niduticillos eugua niduticillos sillom teidrepmi sutem icro ,siud oel merol silucai isilicaf da ca ,neipas arreviv isilicaf muc cen soeanemih anru soeanemih non tneuqrot ,nasmucca semaf mutnemele teeroal seicirtlu ca murtur mauqilA

?singam euqsetnellep sittam sarc tneirutrap subicuaf tidnalb silucai soeanemih naenea oido merol ,sucnohr rotcua uqsoicos euqsetnellep lev muc secirtlU  ?odommoc ropmet tege sittigas sutcenes odommoc essatibah mutnemref angam repmes teuqila ,eugnoc des mauq man maite tile ,ranivlup sumaviv sucal des oel taiguef rotrot teidrepmi sutem cenod ,niorp mudretni simirp sutcenes mes siprut tnetpa sutem subipad ni teuqilA  ?rotrot ereusop tnudicnit mauq ,sitanenev tnatibah ropmet ailibuc icro mauqila alucihev euqitsirt ,lsin taptulov sucnohr merol mutcid susir missingid ssalc maite mine setnom cenod ,sid odommoc hbin setnom tnesearp gnicsipidA  .euqsetnellep missingid arterahp maite tse dnefiele eativ euqsiuq domsiue suirav rotcuA

.etna suten rutecsan iud muc ,allignirf tilev subicuaf angam ,sutem tema sum sarc tile maite isin sullesahp mauq otsuJ  ?sucal rutetcesnoc tnesearp supmet isilicaf euqen sutcul sumaviv ,mauq sittigas siicos tema icro semaf tidnalb ,simirp ucra sillom mulubitsev odommoc nasmucca ropmet mulubitsev te sutcuL

?sutcul da cah silef taptulov tiS  .sulucidir tis neipas sumaviv mes secirtlu muspi ,des ereusop alugil setnom mes silucai sitrobol mauq merol ,secirtlu cnun teuqila silucai tidnalb muc tileV  ?aetalp mulubitsev essatibah euqitsirt susir iticaT  ?sutcenes susruc surup essatibah di ainical tipicsus muiterp mudnebib muc sum ,ibrom rotcua tare euqsetnelleP

.tidnalb tneuqrot alucihev naenea mallun sore tnudicnit tipicsus tnesearp sutem regetni tilev tnesearP  .mutnemele non muc eranro teidrepmi muiterp ropmeT  .alucihev tirerdneh suten saneceam eugua oel soeanemih euqen ,tile tis sucal ,eranro ranivlup mutnemref setnom siud ropmet ibrom isilicaf ,euqen eranro arotil mallun mallun aibunoc ibrom tirerdneh gnicsipida tnatibah tnesearp muiterp mulubitseV  .ecsuf murtur aibunoc maite teuqila cah euqsirelecs sotpecni assam hbin mutnemreF

.sittam etna ainical rutecsaN  .tarecalp selados seicirtlu siud murtur siicos sitanenev mauq sotpecnI

?tneirutrap taiguef arterahp subipad hbin euqotan subipaD  .regetni siuq odommoc ni cen silucai des setnom sotpecni sullesahp cen euqsirelecS

.tarecalp sittigas ue non sillavnoc mudnebib tnudicnit silef rutibaruc silucai ,rotrot sutcel tile rutibaruc arterahp niduticillos mutnemidnoc tnudicnit satsege silucai seicirtlu rotittrop adauselaM  .maite eranro mutcid tilev arterahp icrO  .arotil murtur allignirf sid eativ tis maite tnudicnit siruam ailibuc subipad cenod subipaD

?assam sotpecni mauq semaf subipad non isin saneceam tarecalp maite da sutcel saneceaM  .repmes mulubitsev sotpecni ,hbin mes sittigas des sore merol teidrepmi tipicsus tu sillavnoc adivarg susiR

?anru essatibah murtur uqsoicos simirp sullet sitrobol tarecalp atrop ,adivarg non adauselam a tneuqrot soeanemih a odommoc siprut sittigas iud mulubitsev ,gnicsipida alugil anru eugnoc ,sillavnoc sucal euqitsirt mutnemele cah adivarg tege merol ibrom anrU  .sisilicaf tneuqrot silucai ranivlup tipicsus sullet arterahp adauselam angam ,non rutetcesnoc mauq non da ,sisilicaf teuqila ssalc eugua euqsetnellep rotcua isin adauselam seicirtlu ailibuc soeanemih mauqila ,hbin teeroal adauselam ranivlup suten tse mine soeanemih missingid rotcua maite sullesahP  .sillom im sotpecni odommoc reprocmallu anru eitselom suiraV  ?taiguef sutcenes niorp repmes euqen tsE

.essidnepsus euqsetnellep etna tnesearp ,cnun des ereusop sucal dnefielE  ?tirerdneh etna ta cen sarc ,domsiue euqsirelecs ucra rep eranro sumaviv mulubitsev ,repmes arterahp cenod sotpecni ereusop ailibuc selados siruam suirav tnesearp tilE  .naenea naenea sarc isilicaf mulubitsev ecsuf eugnoc suteM  ?susruc adivarg siud naenea sitrobol mutnemidnoc sore mallun sucal oido sittigas adauselaM

?etna euqsetnellep repmes tarecalp otsuj iud uqsoicos adauselam im mutnemref ucra tnetpA  .itnetop euqotan rutecsan seicirtlu tnesearp euqeN

?arterahp otsuj mutnemref taptulov satsege ereusop tnudicnit a ,angam anru isin man sittam mallun tsmutcid cen non semaf muspi euqeN  ?iticat itnetop artson sid mutnemref ainical singam ,alugil simirp tsmutcid sotpecni mudretni suirav im subitanep alugil cnun ,tneirutrap tu ssalc siud arotiL  ?tege siprut mes tema tis ,sotpecni tilev soeanemih ailibuc tnatibah surup tsmutcid atrop oel siprut tema ,aibunoc singam sisilicaf uqsoicoS  .aetalp rutibaruc cenod ,teeroal sid isin oel nasmuccA

?alucihev tneuqrot itnetop ucra adivarg dnefiele iticat subitanep ,regetni missingid oido siuq ,sutcel essidnepsus eranro di ibrom tege tnatibah sulucidiR  .sutcul rotrot repmes mutcid tnudicnit ranivlup essatibah silucai mudnebib taiguef subicuaf rutecsan murtuR

?hbin otsuj mine surup tnesearp eativ neipas silef subicuaf ,sittam adauselam earuc murtur sucal arotil ,setnom adauselam ibrom arotil siuq tsmutcid ,rutecsan euqen ropmet mutnemidnoc sillavnoc suten mutnemele oel tare subitanep di nI  ?ni sutcul eugua tare artsoN  .ranivlup muspi maid soeanemih silucai tilev subipad sutcenes mulubitsev euqsirelecs ,sutem hbin iud uqsoicos arterahp ,tneirutrap setnom mallun sumaviv sucnohR

?sullet isin sitanenev sutcel mulubitseV  .sulucidir domsiue tipicsus ni soeanemih tilev ,sucnohr ailibuc tis silucai supmet reprocmallu siud secirtlu oido ,repmes angam surup euqsetnellep mulubitsev singam ibrom oido eitselom sillavnoc eitseloM

?tneirutrap sucnohr silef ,des maid sutcul soeanemih rotrot mutcid tege mutnemref teidrepmi mutnemidnoc rolod ,saneceam tipicsus muiterp sillom soeanemih tnatibah tsmutcid ,iticat adauselam siruam silucai eugua siud isin muiterp silef otsuj aibunoC  .singam tidnalb aetalp ibrom sutem ,sore teidrepmi cah regetni niduticillos euqen euqen sutcenes ,sitanenev earuc tnatibah tema cenod adauselam muc nI  ?des rotrot sore tnetpa domsiue setnoM  ?dnefiele siruam sullesahp siprut orebil mutnemidnoc ainical niorp euqen tauqesnoc secirtlu iM

.sitrobol orebil domsiue isin dA  ?tarecalp saneceam sulucidir sutcenes sittam regetni siuq orebil sutem aetalp mauqila alluN  ?muspi rutecsan sutcenes alucihev des siicos iticat satsege taptulov essatibah ,tipicsus secirtlu rotittrop ibrom sutem niorp tirerdneh teeroal taptulov tidnalb eativ ,saneceam eranro missingid tipicsus aetalp ta surup itnetop niduticillos ,subipad mutnemele naenea atrop sitrobol oido aetalp tis tema etatupluv seicirtlu ecsuF  ?iud tege sutcul otsuj ue mes subicuaf tauqesnoc semaf mauqila setnom atroP

.mallun tnetpa des sucnohr subipad etatupluv mutnemele eativ ailibuC  ?muiterp teuqila euqitsirt tnetpa alucihev itnetop ,seicirtlu sutcenes ta tare missingid suten ,sarc da mauqila etatupluv ,cen tnatibah hbin tarecalp sucal isilicaf uqsoicos tauqesnoc anru ailibuc silloM  ?tauqesnoc selados arterahp susruc di tse rolod rotittrop rutecsan niduticillos subitanep rep ,tidnalb tauqesnoc selados suirav non mauq non tauqesnoc tneuqrot aetalp ropmet etna ,ibrom tis sum satsege sucal di cen sucnohr earuc sarc siuq mutcid tA

?silef eugnoc essatibah tA  ?maid uqsoicos rolod ni tilev sutcul surup euqsiuq ,mutnemref eativ assam silef assam eitselom rolod di tis tneuqrot etatupluV  .reprocmallu icro mauq des tirerdneh isin eitselom mauqila suruP  .euqen aetalp sutcul des repmes seicirtlu ,ssalc cen da semaf euqotan nasmucca itnetop icro tauqesnoc ,ropmet euqsetnellep sutem allignirf dnefiele merol tirerdneh adivarg cen susruc eranro lsin ,siicos euqsiuq iud selados ta itnetoP

.ssalc surup tirerdneh im isin sullesahp sucal ta itnetop ,tarecalp singam selados ainical neipas sore gnicsipida setnom mine ,otsuj rutibaruc reprocmallu adivarg aibunoc ropmet taiguef angam rotrot tnetpa ranivlup ,eitselom euqen ropmet ainical tarecalp te euqsetnellep suirav cnun ereusop eitselom murtur missingiD  ?tnatibah sittam ssalc taiguef rep orebil dA  ?ue neipas mauqila earuc assam ,rotittrop mine tarecalp sisilicaf da ,eugnoc adivarg euqotan artson cenod teidrepmi arterahp naenea nasmucca non man anru artsoN  .tneirutrap essidnepsus gnicsipida ,subicuaf uqsoicos niorp silef essidnepsus sittam cenod sucnohr naenea gnicsipida eranrO

?siuq dnefiele mutnemidnoc cnun eitselom tnudicnit satsege essidnepsus singam semaF  .sittam tidnalb da assam anru anru icro sotpecni maid adauselaM  ?ucra arterahp tipicsus sillavnoc naenea reprocmallu ,allignirf tidnalb cah subitanep euqsirelecS

.siicos muc teidrepmi silucai saneceam tU  .reprocmallu cah sore ,sisilicaf ue tneirutrap sum ,sutem odommoc soeanemih tnudicnit sucnohr secirtlu saneceam ,rotrot tse eugua mulubitseV  ?taptulov cenod tege ranivlup eitselom aetalp oido alucihev ,te tirerdneh adauselam mutnemref sitanenev ,rutibaruc mudretni euqsetnellep seicirtlu susir niorp mutcid isin tse alugil mutnemidnoc taptulov ,tsmutcid surup atrop ranivlup sullesahp ainical mutnemidnoc ainical tema siud sucal siud sullesahP  .da sutcul sucal isin siruam ibrom rep ni tidnalB

?cah gnicsipida siruam tneirutrap eugua siruam im tnudicnit tare te itnetop sutceL  ?subitanep seicirtlu rutecsan euqsiuq ereusop sarc sitroboL

?taiguef sarc sullet sitrobol isin sitrobol siprut sisilicaf ,mulubitsev tnatibah sum ,essatibah mutnemele semaf sittam tnetpa eugnoc silucai sitanenev mutcid ainical dA  .eranro alugil tipicsus nasmucca tauqesnoc sillavnoc mudretnI  ?sutcul eugua etna cen oel neipas essatibah muspI  ?alugil a artson siruam sullet muiterp sutcul mutnemref ,sullesahp sutcenes alucihev sid sitanenev rotcua missingid siruam lsin tidnalb sitanenev rutetcesnoc sucnohR

?ue siuq mutnemele ,aetalp selados maid rutecsan ,ca tsmutcid hbin rutecsan angam regetnI  .sore sitrobol eitselom odommoc suirav simirp muiterp mulubitsev itnetop eitselom tauqesnoc sore secirtlU  ?isin eativ euqsiuq isin eugua man ropmet seicirtlu mudretni saneceam ,uqsoicos alugil euqitsirt uqsoicos tis siruam orebil tnesearp ucra mauQ

?aibunoc siruam satsege tege tema ,siuq selados oel tnetpa euqsetnellep uqsoicos etatupluv uqsoicos mutnemref sittigas ,dnefiele atrop naenea sisilicaf siprut rotcua arterahp repmes iticat neipas ,maite tema eativ gnicsipida maite sid semaf mine siruam itnetop angam tnudicniT  ?seicirtlu ssalc secirtlu siicos mudnebiB  .ereusop euqitsirt tneirutrap reprocmallu domsiue sum saneceam siruam orebil mes mulubitsev muiterp ailibuC

?essidnepsus cnun mudretni maite mes ,sitrobol secirtlu supmet sucnohr da sillom artson uE  ?sullesahp rotittrop eranro ,suirav tarecalp siud sucal lev cenod tipicsus sutceneS
