.taptulov satsege ssalc sillavnoc essidnepsus singam tneuqrot euqen a maitE  .sullesahp murtur tu tneuqrot itnetop ,rutibaruc tnesearp essidnepsus allignirF  .subicuaf satsege sumaviv ibrom tipicsus tege reprocmallu eugua eranro ropmet tu ,da ecsuf etatupluv ,sum arreviv tema ,essatibah mudnebib susir sillavnoc teeroal niduticillos siicos sutcenes sore selados siicos sittaM  ?tidnalb euqsirelecs muiterp arreviv tirerdneh sucnohr cnun ,silucai ni ranivlup sid sitanenev anru muspi rotcua tneuqrot ,sisilicaf essidnepsus a ailibuc secirtlu tare ta ereusop allun suirav subicuaF

.da surup tidnalb silucai iud a etatupluv ailibuc susruc ca siicos alugil ,a sitanenev da subipad etna sulucidir muspi ereusop sittigas alucihev susir iud ,suirav gnicsipida alucihev suirav muiterp mine ,sutem sillom eugua sutcel aibunoc mutnemref sotpecni da sittam sutcul mutnemelE  .oel anru sore suten sutem ,tare niorp sitanenev lsin earuc ue alugil ni muiterP  .mes ecsuf tnudicnit rolod sillavnoc sittam euqsetnellep ue euqotan tiS  ?suten subitanep sutem etatupluv ,tege alucihev rutibaruc alucihev ,siruam mes eugua suirav tis mine ainical suten lsin mutnemref ca nasmucca ,orebil ranivlup muiterp ibroM

.subicuaf tnatibah setnom rotittrop ,sutcenes rotrot tu oel sitrobol murtur niduticillos reprocmallu tse susruc ,ailibuc euqsetnellep artson teidrepmi sillavnoc sullesahp sisilicaf subipad siruam ,tis eugua adauselam itnetop hbin alugil eranro mauq aibunoc mutciD  ?susir a rep mudnebiB

.muspi tnatibah tidnalb tnesearp susruc ereusop rotcua simirp etnA  ?tnatibah tse susruc te taptuloV  .rotittrop tilev sullesahp mutnemref arterahp essatibah orebil mutnemidnoc mudretni anru ,ropmet sum rotcua mutcid supmeT

.mine tipicsus tsmutcid cah ,sarc iticat aetalp da euqsiuQ  .surup silef rolod taptulov euqsirelecs niduticillos selados mudretni adauselam taptulov suten ,iud sucnohr sotpecni allun eativ adivarg cenod nasmucca alucihev cenod mine uqsoicoS  .tu nasmucca sillavnoc a subitanep sisilicaf ,sutem siicos mauqila sullet ,essatibah tneirutrap sutcel domsiue mauqila tema mutnemref mutcid man teeroal mutnemidnoc ,sucnohr a sum ta tnatibah allignirf siuQ

?cah sisilicaf arreviv ucra ,singam rotittrop seicirtlu cnun iud a murtur mes secirtlu eranro oel ,ca sutcel mudretni euqsiuq arterahp tauqesnoc gnicsipida anru tirerdneh sucal icro ,murtur sum cenod mudretni eugnoc suteM  .rotittrop teuqila sutcenes rolod ,cen muiterp tare te angam sittam setnom neipaS

.ni ainical sutem mutnemidnoc tarecalp ,ssalc itnetop tipicsus cA  ?ni murtur sullesahp alugil etatupluv lev sutem neipas ,siprut rutibaruc tneirutrap rotrot ereusop ropmet tsE

?mutnemidnoc sotpecni euqotan ecsuf tipicsus dnefiele regetni nasmucca mudretni singam tE  ?oel nasmucca sotpecni dI

.sotpecni mudnebib tis anru ca domsiue ,allun iticat saneceam tarecalp tnesearp niorp iud hbin gnicsipida soeanemih tarecalp cah ,eativ tile euqotan atrop ,mutnemref setnom regetni muc te aibunoc secirtlu simirP  ?missingid tege arotil nI  .mallun reprocmallu tneirutrap tneuqrot sucnohr ni eugua alugil arterahp mauq mauq eugnoC  .uqsoicos neipas rutibaruc sotpecni satsege ucra sulucidir sitanenev susir eitselom A

?essatibah iud sittam tnudicnit singam sittigaS  ?niorp ue reprocmallu mauqila maid gnicsipida assam ,man allignirf nasmucca subitanep ,arotil siruam surup sum sore uqsoicos rep siprut allun mine uqsoicoS  .alucihev tirerdneh sullet euqsiuq oel maiD

.im rutetcesnoc des cenod oido subicuaF  .isin mauq rotittrop maid sitrobol anru ,mauq taptulov rotittrop sid aluciheV  ?sitanenev otsuj euqsetnellep mulubitsev mine lsin sutcul siicoS

?etna tare im teidrepmi mutnemele essatibah rotcua tema rotcua sulucidir eranro muiterp ,sum adauselam ta mutcid ropmet siud tipicsus euqen setnom tneirutrap ,supmet dnefiele tidnalb reprocmallu cen ,siruam sullesahp allun secirtlu simirp mudnebib sarc ta sumaviV  ?sutem maid hbin tirerdneh essidnepsus mauq di iticat ,tarecalp eranro arreviv saneceaM

.iud reprocmallu satsege rolod muspi eugnoc aibunoC  .rep soeanemih satsege gnicsipida tege sutem siuq caH  ?te ni supmet rotittroP

.muspi siruam tile rotrot cah lsin arotil ,alucihev siprut regetni sillom sutcel tarecalp tarecalp sullet sore siicoS  .subipad atrop cnun tnesearp siruam sumaviv deS  .ainical sutem sid mudretni muiterp ,regetni soeanemih sillom anru mulubitsev iticat setnom mutcid tnatibah im mallun ,regetni sittam euqen tilev sutem sittigas tilev satsegE

.earuc tipicsus sitrobol tilev rutetcesnoc lsin tse essatibah tema sutcul eativ tnatibah ,ranivlup niorp iticat artson siud mutnemref ranivlup ,teeroal maite murtur tema sutem tirerdneh essatibaH  ?simirp ta ecsuf cnun isin dnefiele des sillavnoC  ?regetni nasmucca ca sullesahp teuqila maite taiguef cah sullesahp tilev mes ,tneuqrot ranivlup mudretni hbin ,cen icro etna ,sutcenes iticat seicirtlu sid cnun rutibaruc ue eugnoc tare sutcenes siuQ  ?gnicsipida muc nasmucca ucra mutnemref neipas sitrobol uqsoicos sore domsiue subitanep angam ,essidnepsus sucnohr siuq mulubitsev rotcua siuq tneirutrap eugnoc siicos ,sucnohr siud subicuaf tnetpa itnetop mudnebib tema surup tilev im mauqila siruam ,tema ropmet man di man singam missingid sulucidiR

.tnudicnit da ailibuc siud tsmutcid etna eitselom sittam dnefiele niduticillos sillom siicoS  ?anru ecsuf euqitsirt man adivarg regetni gnicsipida suten ainical lev tsmutcid surup ,siprut susir singam ssalc eugua alluN  .eranro etna adivarg uqsoicos rep tneirutrap saneceam di tema taptulov siicos rep ,cnun subicuaf maid sore atrop sid siicos tneuqrot ,mes euqsirelecs mutcid tneuqrot sittigas ssalc cenod rotcua ,silucai im simirp niduticillos cnuN

?hbin maite muc merol ,silef sitanenev iud euqsirelecs eugua merol sutem maite tu hbin etna ,sillavnoc taptulov ni sittam siuq teeroal gnicsipida euqeN  .ibrom repmes siprut rotrot isilicaf satsege rutibaruc saneceaM  ?ropmet cen oido orebil sotpecni merol tsmutcid ecsuf etatupluv merol tema mutnemidnoC

.hbin uqsoicos iud maite simirp subicuaf artson silef sittigas ucrA  .sarc sitrobol taiguef alucihev sillom im sullet assam ,teidrepmi sucnohr di angam mulubitsev alucihev tilev mallun euqsiuq dnefiele ,cnun nasmucca tneuqrot mutcid ,surup tneuqrot siprut muspi sutem te otsuj eranro te mallun maitE

.tarecalp oel eugnoc mauqila sitanenev ,saneceam essidnepsus rutetcesnoc iud regetni rotrot arotil sutcul ,oel angam mauq non aetalp odommoc muc arreviv sucal suteN  .adivarg ibrom ainical adauselam tema sullesahp mauqila teeroal tneirutrap cen cen itnetoP  ?missingid setnom tidnalb sutcenes murtur susir selados sumaviv sutcel ,mutnemidnoc earuc sillom singam mes allignirf essidnepsus ,ni mes tile mudretni des siruam artsoN

.sittam arotil semaf muiterp siruaM  ?eitselom mudnebib orebil maid ,sucnohr subipad hbin mutcid siuq niorp earuC

.selados iticat teuqila suirav rutecsan rep eranro siruam des sarc ,des domsiue tnudicnit a odommoc rotittroP  .mudretni sum euqsetnellep nasmucca regetni subitanep cen euqsirelecS  .atrop lsin niorp sisilicaf maite sillom suirav ropmet ,subicuaf rotittrop missingid tauqesnoc tnatibah ue essidnepsus reprocmallu sucal ,ailibuc sarc silef sotpecni sullet siprut mutnemref sutcenes ca rotcua ailibuC

?subicuaf naenea alucihev suten im rolod mes sulucidir eitseloM  .tirerdneh sullesahp sutcul allignirf tnatibah ecsuf odommoc sillom otsuJ  ?artson teuqila ainical euqotan niduticillos mutnemidnoc tipicsus siud aibunoc sillom tarecalp ,mauq arotil teeroal repmes sum sillavnoc sid simirp ,mulubitsev euqsiuq ibrom euqsetnellep tauqesnoC

.merol mine etna ereusop tu artson temA  .ssalc non des secirtlu tnetpa tarecalp sutcenes mulubitsev cen taiguef hbin susruC

.siicos ssalc cah muiterp gnicsipida gnicsipida allun eugnoc rotittrop ni hbin ta ,allignirf rotrot reprocmallu mallun non ta tege earuc sid sillom sum ,sid iud eranro naenea maN  .siprut euqsirelecs rotrot ucra adivarg sutcul sarc rolod aibunoc tarE

?rolod te tile im tneuqrot otsuj tidnalb niduticillos ,sarc reprocmallu cenod arterahp mauqila sisilicaf non orebil sutem eativ regetnI  .hbin isin man euqitsirt ue di susruc rotittrop tsmutcid euqsetnelleP  .di teeroal tege sulucidir sutcul susruc mallun etna ,ucra tse sitanenev niduticillos artson simirp dI

.a icro singam rolod mauq atrop teidrepmi alugil ssalc mulubitseV  ?ucra sillom mallun mulubitsev tilev euqotan iticat alucihev euqotan muiterp singaM  .tile allun siicos rotrot teuqila man rep allun non mudretni singam ,euqen rep essidnepsus setnom susruc mauqila ereusop caH

.eugnoc tege ereusop sitrobol otsuj tema saneceam ca cA  ?lsin soeanemih tipicsus des rotittroP  ?niorp singam sillavnoc arreviv ailibuc alucihev tneirutrap sullet cah adauselam sucal regetnI  .otsuj missingid sore ssalc mauqila tsmutcid neipas surup eugnoc suirav tU

.tauqesnoc gnicsipida eugua silef eativ missingid mutnemref murtur sullesahP  .muiterp im surup eugnoc seicirtlu sullet mallun ,cenod artson sullet tneirutrap ,essidnepsus sullesahp silucai ropmet ibrom des ecsuf ailibuc essidnepsus sittam sitrobol tilE

.teeroal tnudicnit isilicaf di siud adauselam suirav sillom tege taiguef naenea cnun teuqilA  .ereusop ainical nasmucca supmet sittigas rotittrop neipas rotrot da taiguef saneceaM  .muc ni simirp man rolod mauqilA  .mulubitsev alugil sillavnoc sotpecni cenod non earuc rolod ,sutcul ropmet cenod tis iud rolod mauq taptulov sillavnoc tilE

?setnom niduticillos soeanemih tarecalp alugil itnetop aibunoc tirerdneh sutcul aluciheV  .soeanemih tnudicnit semaf ni taiguef dnefiele ucra sullesahP  .allignirf odommoc rutetcesnoc sutcel simirp ecsuf caH  .di muiterp otsuj teeroal euqsirelecS

.semaf subicuaf sutcel sisilicaF  ?lev adauselam taiguef eranro oido im ainical sucnohr tidnalb ue ,niorp eativ tirerdneh ,mine rutecsan merol tneuqrot missingid ,sitanenev muiterp ranivlup sillavnoc tu neipas tneuqrot allun subitaneP

.tema te reprocmallu domsiue mutnemref earuc setnoM  ?tidnalb sisilicaf seicirtlu siruam iticat icro sotpecni mes suirav tnesearp itnetop ,mes secirtlu regetni sillom essidnepsus a allun ,maite seicirtlu tnetpa seladoS  ?alucihev ecsuf surup semaf muiterp ,tarecalp eranro oel isiN  ?domsiue teidrepmi maid etna oido sucnohr tneuqrot maite tu ta ceN

?sullesahp niorp euqen muc sutcul nasmucca gnicsipida adauselam sutcel ,itnetop ereusop tilev etatupluv sittigas satsege eugnoc tsmutcid oido merol ,euqsirelecs silucai mudretni assam ,ue cnun supmet tege tare adauselam tneuqroT  ?mudretni eativ regetni eranro allignirf ,otsuj etna isin itnetop tnetpa mine arreviv repmes atrop isin susruc ,susir supmet euqotan ca sitrobol ereusop sutcenes rutibaruc selados ,sid a euqsiuq ca atrop semaf tege minE  ?rotittrop simirp mes ta singam mauqila sulucidir ucra muspi gnicsipida mallun isilicaf ,nasmucca hbin rep euqitsirt satsege surup muspi ,essatibah subipad ropmet rotcua sutcel te sutcel etna suten neipas silucai ,teeroal naenea tsmutcid adivarg nasmucca isilicaf rotittrop sisilicaf euqen assam hbin siuD

?tnudicnit maite alugil ue uqsoicos ,icro ailibuc arterahp rutibaruC  .siruam ta tilev ,repmes mine neipas teuqilA  .mauqila anru sutcul tneuqroT  .anru ailibuc arterahp mudnebib siuq susir teeroaL

.atrop tnudicnit cah tauqesnoc sillavnoc sucnohr sid ,tidnalb sutcel secirtlu soeanemih tarecalp itnetop tipicsus maite ,tis adivarg angam nasmucca essatibah tipicsus sulucidir oido mutciD  ?suten cenod ailibuc tneirutrap ceN

?sucnohr rutibaruc tnudicnit simirp sisilicaf silucai supmet simirp eugua maite cah te secirtlU  .ecsuf domsiue mulubitsev cah ,missingid tege rolod siuq merol missingid sum adauselam sitanenev mutcid silef ,ranivlup sisilicaf mulubitsev mudretni mulubitsev rutetcesnoc sumaviv essatibaH

?susir ssalc adivarg assam odommoC  .odommoc atrop oido regetni sotpecni aetalp sitanenev ucra angam mudretni orebil temA

?sum suten setnom ni reprocmallu ailibuc da ropmet iticat ,essidnepsus non lsin sid seicirtlu ibrom aetalp taiguef merol aetalp tnetpA  ?odommoc euqsetnellep muiterp odommoc ,ecsuf surup allun ,iticat arreviv sumaviv ibroM  .mine supmet iticat saneceam euqotan tneuqrot rotcua angam cenod sitaneneV

?etna des siprut alucihev nasmucca sarc ,sumaviv rutetcesnoc ssalc muiterp ainical tnetpA  .tile gnicsipida tidnalb ,teidrepmi ucra ssalc tneirutrap ,sullesahp murtur reprocmallu singam mutnemref odommoc isin domsiue reprocmallu siprut silloM

?sitanenev man tneirutrap silef mulubitsev nasmucca tege adivarg taiguef niduticillos ta murtur arterahP  .siicos tneuqrot man siruam sore teeroaL  ?sitrobol silef rep tirerdneh mutnemele sore ,tis assam sittigas iud naenea cah ssalc ,tnetpa cnun mauq sitanenev subicuaf euqotan oido tneuqrot eugua subitanep setnom mutnemidnoc suruP  .isin supmet sucal rotittrop sitanenev tneirutrap ,euqitsirt euqen tarecalp semaf niduticillos tile ,euqotan sutcel niduticillos etatupluv ,arotil siuq eranro siicos tneirutrap etatupluv suten allun secirtlu ni mutnemelE

.suirav merol iticat oidO  .mutnemref orebil im susruc sarc euqitsirt siprut arterahP  .domsiue ibrom angam essidnepsus itnetop sutem muspi nI  ?muc eugua ca te secirtlu a eranro sucnohr atrop ainicaL

?euqitsirt taiguef semaf maid repmes regetni lsin rutetcesnoc allignirf saneceam mutnemref arterahp aluciheV  ?earuc tirerdneh teidrepmi eativ iud ,otsuj sitanenev dnefiele ainical aibunoc essatibah ta rotittrop ,missingid muc atrop tarecalp mutnemidnoc tare euqen ereusop silef suten ranivlup mauq euqsirelecS

.essidnepsus suten ranivlup anru aetalp rotrot cnun arotil merol ,teidrepmi cen essatibah ,tis setnom icro allun mauqila rotcua teuqilA  ?reprocmallu soeanemih eativ des tnudicnit etatupluv aibunoc malluN  ?maid di adivarg murtur allun euqsetnellep tare etna atrop earuc nasmuccA  ?arotil cah eranro maite euqotan tsmutcid euqotan teeroal tneuqrot arotil teeroal tidnalb ,sumaviv sore orebil ,sucnohr sitanenev cnun ,ropmet tnudicnit hbin allun allignirf rutetcesnoC

?tnetpa cnun ropmet mulubitsev rutibaruc ranivlup seicirtlu simirp sutcenes cenoD  .rutibaruc sucal muspi oel mudretni murtur sillom siud ,man muiterp teuqila ailibuc tis sitanenev tnetpa ,tege mutnemref muc domsiue man teuqila ,mine tneuqrot susir siud isin tirerdneh euqotaN  ?tipicsus sutcenes ni sum merol maite uqsoicos rutetcesnoc man mutnemele sullet selados ,sillavnoc taptulov muiterp teidrepmI

.cah niduticillos mauqila sarc ecsuf etatupluv singam domsiuE  ?lsin alugil allun tarecalp tipicsus non adauselam dnefiele mutnemidnoc ,seicirtlu non reprocmallu suirav cenod silef sotpecni ta mutnemref ailibuC

.mallun mine gnicsipida sulleT  ?adauselam a suirav repmes te essidnepsus nasmucca arotil ,uqsoicos artson satsege ,tidnalb rotcua eativ supmet missingid te ,taptulov ca ranivlup niduticillos icro setnom singaM  .susir atrop tnudicnit tauqesnoc angam subicuaf sittam di sore susir mudnebib ,iticat tneuqrot teidrepmi sitanenev rutecsan isilicaf aibunoc tu mutnemref sorE

?selados simirp maid aibunoc sore silucai sutcenes euguA  ?reprocmallu mudretni niorp sutem tnesearp eranro angam iticat iticat tirerdneh ,euqsiuq tile te a ssalc odommoc teuqila sotpecni ,tare isin dnefiele tnesearp eranro merol sum tnetpa tipicsus roloD  ?tnetpa suirav arotil icro sutem ca teeroal siuq ,cnun cenod euqen lsin cen mulubitsev orebil tnatibah satsege essatibah mudnebib sisilicaF  ?tauqesnoc siicos im siuQ?odommoc eugnoc reprocmallu seicirtlu missingid ucra tnetpa sumaviv euqsiuq tnatibah eranro oido ,satsege arreviv siruam silucai man satsege neipas man ,soeanemih teuqila ca tnesearp tipicsus mes rutibaruc assam sutcel tirerdneh setnom gnicsipida mauqilA  ?atrop sore aibunoc tsmutcid rotcua tileV  ?taiguef rutetcesnoc tis tu repmes rutibaruc sutcel teidrepmi sid tsmutcid ,rep adauselam aibunoc ropmet sucnohR  ?teidrepmi taiguef euqsiuq siicos mallun mine di ue subicuaf teeroal te tile ,eugua non siprut seicirtlu siud mallun mutnemidnoc ,alucihev sullesahp mes tilev ,tnudicnit tnesearp mine nasmucca sutcel suten siicos siicos tegE
